## 祆教 / 琐罗亚斯德教

### —— 1. Khshnaothra ——
Khshnaothra Ahurahe Mazdāo.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 2. Niyyat / Dibache ——
Pa nām i yazdān, Ohrmazd Khodāe awazūnī.

为明日上线一切顺利、部署平安、无 P0 事故；愿此事行于 Asha，不夺他人福报，不损他人寿数，不以他人受害为成就；愿善思、善言、善行护持一切相关之人、系统与事务。

Humata hukhta hvarshta andar Asha.

### —— 3. Kem Na Mazda ——
Kêm-nâ mazdâ mavaitê pâyûm dadå,  
hyat mâ dregvå dîdareshatâ aênanghê,  
anyêm thwahmât âthrascâ mananghascâ,  
ýayå shyaothanâish ashem thraoshtâ ahurâ,  
tãm môi dãstvãm daênayâi frâvaocâ.  

Kê verethrem-jâ thwâ pôi sêñghâ ýôi heñtî,  
cithrâ môi dãm ahûmbish ratûm cizhdî,  
at hôi vohû seraoshô jañtû mananghâ,  
mazdâ ahmâi ýahmâi vashî kahmâicît.  

Pâta-nô tbishyañtat pairi mazdåsca ârmaitishca speñtasca,  
nase daêvî druxsh, nase daêvô-cithre, nase daêvô-frakarshte, nase daêvô-fradâiti,  
apa druxsh nase, apa druxsh dvâra, apa druxsh vînase, apâxedhre apa-nasyehe,  
mâ mereñcainîsh gaêthå astvaitîsh ashahe,  
nemascâ ýâ ârmaitish îzhâcâ.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 4. Patet / Ahura Mazda Khodāe ——
Ahura-Mazda khodāe, Ahereman awā-dashãn, dur avāz dāshtār, zad shekasteh bād.  

Ahura-Mazda khodāe, az hamā gunāh patet pashemānum,  
az harvastīn dushmata duzhukhta duzhvarshta,  
mem pa getī manīd, oem goft, oem kard, oem jast, oem būn būd ested.  

Az ān gunāh, manashnī gavashnī kunashnī, tanī ravānī getī minōānī,  
okhe awākhsh pashemān, pa se gavashnī pa patet hom.

### —— 5. Jasa me Avanghe Mazda / Fravarane ——
Jasa me avanghe Mazda. Jasa me avanghe Mazda. Jasa me avanghe Mazda.  

Mazdayasnō ahmī, Mazdayasnō Zarathushtrish fravarānē āstūtascā fravaretascā.  
Āstuyē humatem manō, āstuyē hūkhtem vachō, āstuyē hvarshtem shyaothanem.  
Āstuyē daēnām vanguhīm Māzdayasnīm,  
fraspāyaokhedhrām, nidhāsnaithishem, khvaētvadathām ashaonīm,  
yā hāitināmchā būshyeintināmchā mazishtāchā vahishtāchā sraēshtāchā,  
yā āhūirish Zarathushtrish.  
Ahurāi Mazdāi vīspā vohū chinahmī.  
Aēshā astī daēnayāo Māzdayasnōish āstūitish.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 6. 核心 manthra ——
Yathā ahū vairyō, athā ratush ashāt-chit hachā,  
vanghēush dazdā mananghō, shyaothananām anghēush Mazdāi,  
xshathremchā Ahurāi ā, yim drigubyō dadat vāstārem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

Yenghē hātām āat yesnē paiti vanghō,  
Mazdāo Ahurō vaēthā ashāt hachā,  
yāonghāmchā tāschā tāschā yazamaidē.

### —— 7. 正行：上线与部署平安 ——
Sraoshahe ashyehe, takhmahe, tanu-manthrahe, darshi-draosh ahuiryehe,  
khshnaothra yasnaicha vahmaicha khshnaothraicha frasastayaecha.  

Yasnemcha vahmemcha aojascha zavarecha āfrīnāmi,  
Verethraghnahe Ahuradhātahe vanaintyāoscha uparatātō.

愿明日上线之事，离混乱、离疏失、离重大事故；愿所当发现者及时显明，所当修正者得以修正，所当协作者以善思善言善行相助；愿部署平安，事务在 Asha 中完成。

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 8. Ahmai Raeshcha / Doa Tan-Dorosti ——
Ahmāi raēshcha khvarenanghacha,  
Ahmāi tanvō drvatātem,  
Ahmāi tanvō vazdvārē,  
Ahmāi tanvō verethrem,  
Ahmāi ishtim pourush-khathrem,  
Ahmāi asnāmchit frazantim,  
Ahmāi darekham darekho-jītim,  
Ahmāi vahishtem ahum ashaonām,  
raochanghem vispō-khathrem.

Tandarosti, dorosti, zor, niru, khoreh, awazuni,  
ravāni shād, tan dorost, geti minōānī andar Asha,  
为明日上线一切顺利、部署平安、无 P0 事故 rāy.

Ahmāi raēshcha; Hazanghrem; Jasa me Avanghe Mazda; Kerfeh Mozd.

Yathā ahū vairyō, athā ratush ashāt-chit hachā,  
vanghēush dazdā mananghō, shyaothananām anghēush Mazdāi,  
xshathremchā Ahurāi ā, yim drigubyō dadat vāstārem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 9. 回结悔净与护持 ——
Āstuyē humatem manō, āstuyē hūkhtem vachō, āstuyē hvarshtem shyaothanem.  
Az hamā gunāh patet pashemānum.  

Mazdayasnō ahmī, Mazdayasnō Zarathushtrish fravarānē.  
Ahurāi Mazdāi vīspā vohū chinahmī.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

## 神智学协会

In quietness of mind and goodwill of heart, in the name of the One Life, and for the good of the whole human family, this prayer is held for tomorrow’s launch and deployment: may all go smoothly, may the deployment be safe, and may there be no P0 incident, within right human relations and the Plan of Love and Light.

From the point of Light within the Mind of God  
Let light stream forth into the minds of men.  
Let Light descend on Earth.

From the point of Love within the Heart of God  
Let love stream forth into the hearts of men.  
May Christ return to Earth.

From the centre where the Will of God is known  
Let purpose guide the little wills of men—  
The purpose which the Masters know and serve.

From the centre which we call the race of men  
Let the Plan of Love and Light work out  
And may it seal the door where evil dwells.

Let Light and Love and Power restore the Plan on Earth.

May clarity guide every decision, steadiness uphold every hand, and right cooperation prevail among all who serve this event. May obstacles be removed without harm to any person; may success not dispossess, diminish, or injure others; may no will be coerced and no harm be returned.

May this intention remain within the universal goodwill of Light, Love, Power, and the Plan, free from selfish grasping, sectarian division, or control of another’s will. May the benefit of this safe and peaceful deployment be dedicated to right human relations, to responsible service, and to the welfare of all beings.

## Reclaiming（Starhawk）

Ground of being, Earth below and within,  
I center in breath, body, and presence.  
I feel my feet upon the living Earth,  
my spine as the world-tree,  
my breath as tide and wind.

By my will, by my breath, by my truth,  
this circle is cast here and now,  
a boundary of clarity, consent, and love.

East, powers of Air:  
breath, song, thought, and dawn,  
be present in this circle.  
Bring clear communication, clean signals, and alert minds.

South, powers of Fire:  
will, courage, heat, and transformation,  
be present in this circle.  
Bring steady action, decisive care, and resilient resolve.

West, powers of Water:  
feeling, dream, grief, and healing,  
be present in this circle.  
Bring calm response, wise flow, and quick restoration.

North, powers of Earth:  
body, root, stone, and bread,  
be present in this circle.  
Bring stable systems, sound foundations, and grounded hands.

Goddess, immanent one,  
She who is within and around all beings,  
be present in this circle.  
Sacred web of life, living power-with,  
be present in this work.

Air I am,  
Fire I am,  
Water, Earth, and Spirit I am.

For tomorrow’s launch,  
for a smooth going-live,  
for safe deployment,  
for no P0 incidents,  
for all who build, review, monitor, respond, and depend on this work,  
I raise this prayer.

Let the gathered will around tomorrow’s release  
rise as a cone of power,  
not to dominate,  
not to force any will,  
not to take good from any other,  
but to strengthen courage, clarity, protection, and shared good.

She changes everything She touches,  
and everything She touches changes.

Let the code be clear.  
Let the build be steady.  
Let the deployment path be open.  
Let hidden faults be revealed before harm is done.  
Let alerts be meaningful, dashboards truthful, logs readable, and rollback paths ready.  
Let hands be calm, minds awake, and communication kind.  
Let every dependency, service, pipeline, network, database, queue, cache, and configuration  
stand in right relation for this release.

Let coercion fall away.  
Let fear be named and released.  
Let power-over be undone.  
Let power-with arise.  
Let this work be aligned with consent, justice, healing, and the freedom of all beings concerned.

Earth my body,  
Water my blood,  
Air my breath,  
and Fire my spirit.

She changes everything She

## 瑟勒玛（Thelema）

Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.

Under the Law of Thelema, in the matter of tomorrow’s go-live, deployment, and release into service, let this word be set in harmony with True Will.

ΑΠΟ ΠΑΝΤΟΣ ΚΑΚΟΔΑΙΜΟΝΟΣ.

ΣΟΙ, Ὦ ΦΑΛΛΕ, ἸΣΧΥΡΟΣ, ΕΥΧΑΡΙΣΤΟΣ, ΙΑΩ.

ΘΗΡΙΟΝ.

ΝΥΙΤ.

ΒΑΒΑΛΟΝ.

ΑΔΙΤ.

ΙΩ ΠΑΝ.

ΠΡΟ ΜΟΥ ΙΥΓΓΕΣ,  
ΟΠΙΣΩ ΜΟΥ ΤΕΛΕΤΑΡΧΑΙ,  
ΕΠΙ ΔΕΞΙΑ ΣΥΝΟΧΕΣ,  
ΕΠΑΡΙΣΤΕΡΑ ΔΑΙΜΟΝΕΣ,  
ΦΛΕΓΕΙ ΓΑΡ ΠΕΡΙ ΜΟΥ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ΠΕΝΤΕ,  
ΚΑΙ ΕΝ ΤΗΙ ΣΤΗΛΗΙ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ἙΞ ἙΣΤΗΚΕ.

Hail unto Thee who art Ra in Thy rising, even unto Thee who art Ra in Thy strength, who travellest over the Heavens in Thy bark at the Uprising of the Sun. Tahuti standeth in His splendour at the prow, and Ra-Hoor abideth at the helm. Hail unto Thee from the Abodes of Night!

Unity uttermost showed!  
I adore the might of Thy breath,  
Supreme and terrible God,  
Who makest the gods and death  
To tremble before Thee:—  
I, I adore thee!

Appear on the throne of Ra!  
Open the ways of the Khu!  
Lighten the ways of the Ka!  
The ways of the Khabs run through  
To stir me or still me!  
Aum! let it fill me!

Let tomorrow’s go-live be ordered according to True Will: the deployment stable, the paths clear, the services sound, the signals timely, the rollback and safeguards ready, and no P0 incident arising.

Let this success seek no restriction of another star, no deprivation of another’s due, and no shortening or harm of any life; let obstacles be removed without injury, confusion be dispelled without coercion, and the work proceed in right measure.

ΑΠΟ ΠΑΝΤΟΣ ΚΑΚΟΔΑΙΜΟΝΟΣ.  
ΦΛΕΓΕΙ ΓΑΡ ΠΕΡΙ ΜΟΥ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ΠΕΝΤΕ,  
ΚΑΙ ΕΝ ΤΗΙ ΣΤΗΛΗΙ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ἙΞ ἙΣΤΗΚΕ.

Love is the law, love under will.

## 玛丁主义（Martinism）

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Seigneur, Dieu éternel, source de toute lumière, de toute justice et de toute miséricorde,  
que notre pensée, notre parole et notre acte soient redressés devant Toi.  
Seigneur Jésus-Christ, Réparateur, que ta paix descende sur l’œuvre qui doit être mise en ligne demain,  
et sur l’intention droite nommée devant Toi.

愿明日上线一切顺利，部署平安，诸环节得以清明有序；若有隐患，愿其在不伤害任何人的方式中显明、止息、修正，无 P0 事故。此愿不求夺取他人福分，不求转嫁损失于他人，只愿在真理、谨慎、慈爱与正当秩序中成就。

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum magnam misericordiam tuam.  
Et secundum multitudinem miserationum tuarum, dele iniquitatem meam.  
Amplius lava me ab iniquitate mea,  
et a peccato meo munda me.  
Cor mundum crea in me, Deus,  
et spiritum rectum innova in visceribus meis.  
Ne proicias me a facie tua,  
et Spiritum sanctum tuum ne auferas a me.  
Redde mihi laetitiam salutaris tui,  
et spiritu principali confirma me.

Asperges me, Domine, hyssopo, et mundabor;  
lavabis me, et super nivem dealbabor.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

In principio erat Verbum,  
et Verbum erat apud Deum,  
et Deus erat Verbum.  
Hoc erat in principio apud Deum.  
Omnia per ipsum facta sunt:  
et sine ipso factum est nihil, quod factum est.  
In ipso vita erat,  
et vita erat lux hominum:  
et lux in tenebris lucet,  
et tenebrae eam non comprehenderunt.

Domine Deus providentiae,  
ordinem, lucem et pacem infunde in hoc opus crastinum.  
Quod confusum est, dirige;  
quod occultum periculosum est, manifesta ante ruinam;  
quod fragile est, confirma;  
quod superfluum est, remove sine damno.  
Non per voluntatem propriam, non per superbiam, non per violentiam,  
sed secundum voluntatem tuam,  
fiat rectitudo in consilio, vigilantia in manibus,  
patientia in corde, pax in exitu.

Seigneur Jésus-Christ, Réparateur,  
que l’intérieur temple soit gardé dans le silence,  
que la lumière divine éclaire le jugement,  
que toute parole vaine retourne au silence,  
que toute intention impure soit consumée dans la miséricorde divine,  
et que l’œuvre soit réintégrée dans l’ordre, la vérité et la charité.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum magnam misericordiam tuam.  
Cor mundum crea in me, Deus,  
et spiritum rectum innova in visceribus meis.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

## Spiritism · Kardecism（凯德克派）

Dieu tout-puissant, souverainement juste et bon,  
que ta volonté soit faite et non la nôtre.  
Si la demande que nous formons est utile aux âmes concernées,  
conforme à ta loi, à la charité et à la justice,  
daigne l’accueillir avec miséricorde.

Notre Père qui êtes aux cieux,  
que votre nom soit sanctifié;  
que votre règne arrive;  
que votre volonté soit faite sur la terre comme au ciel.  
Donnez-nous aujourd’hui notre pain de chaque jour;  
pardonnez-nous nos offenses,  
comme nous pardonnons à ceux qui nous ont offensés;  
ne nous laissez pas succomber à la tentation,  
mais délivrez-nous du mal.  
Ainsi soit-il.

Bons Esprits qui êtes les ministres de Dieu,  
assistez-nous dans l’épreuve présente.  
Anges gardiens, Esprits protecteurs,  
éclairez notre pensée, soutenez notre courage,  
écartez de nous les pensées mauvaises,  
et inspirez-nous ce qui est juste, prudent, charitable  
et conforme à la loi de Dieu.

Seigneur,  
nous te prions pour la mise en ligne de demain:  
que le déploiement se fasse dans le calme, avec ordre et lucidité;  
que les vérifications nécessaires soient accomplies avec soin;  
que les erreurs cachées soient aperçues à temps;  
que les personnes responsables gardent sang-froid, entraide et discernement;  
et qu’aucun accident grave, aucun incident de priorité critique,  
ne vienne nuire aux usagers ni accabler injustement quiconque.

Mon Dieu, inspirez-nous la meilleure résolution  
dans cette circonstance.  
Bons Esprits qui nous protégez,  
aidez-nous à discerner ce qui est conforme à la prudence,  
à la justice, à l’humilité et au bien commun.  
Que cette réussite ne soit pas demandée au détriment d’autrui;  
qu’elle ne dépouille personne, ne blesse personne,  
et ne serve ni l’orgueil, ni l’intérêt égoïste,  
mais l’accomplissement loyal du devoir.

Nous prions aussi pour tous les vivants concernés par cet événement:  
pour ceux qui développent, relisent, déploient, surveillent et décident;  
pour ceux qui utiliseront le service;  
pour ceux qui pourraient être inquiets, fatigués ou sous pression.  
Que les bons Esprits les entourent,  
qu’ils leur inspirent patience, clarté, coopération,  
et le courage de réparer sans orgueil ce qui doit être réparé.

S’il se présente une difficulté,  
préserve-nous du découragement, de la colère et de l’accusation injuste.  
Apprends-nous à reconnaître nos fautes,  
à demander pardon lorsque nous avons manqué,  
à pardonner les manquements d’autrui,  
et à transformer cette expérience en progrès moral.

Seigneur,  
ne permets pas que cette prière serve la curiosité frivole,  
la domination d’aucune créature visible ou invisible,  
ni l’attente d’un prodige sans effort.  
Qu’elle soit seulement un acte de foi,  
de charité, de repentir, de vigilance  
et de soumission à ta volonté.

Que tout bien accompli soit rapporté à Dieu,  
source de toute justice et de toute bonté.  
Ainsi soit-il.

---

## Spiritualism / NSAC

Infinite Intelligence, God of love, law, and life,  
I come in reverence, in sincerity, and in personal responsibility,  
holding tomorrow’s online launch, peaceful deployment, and freedom from P0 incidents before Thee.

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

I affirm:  
We believe in Infinite Intelligence.  
We believe that the phenomena of Nature, both physical and spiritual,  
are the expression of Infinite Intelligence.  
We affirm that true religion is living in obedience to Nature’s Laws.  
We affirm that the existence and personal identity of the individual  
continue after the change called death.  
We affirm that communication with the so-called dead is a fact,  
scientifically proven by the phenomena of Spiritualism.  
We affirm the highest morality contained in the Golden Rule:  
Therefore all things whatsoever ye would that men should do to you,  
do ye even so to them.  
We affirm moral responsibility, and that each soul makes its own happiness  
or unhappiness as it obeys or disobeys Nature’s physical and spiritual laws.  
We affirm that the doorway to reformation is never closed  
against any soul here or hereafter.  
We affirm that the precepts of Prophecy and Healing are Divine attributes  
proven through Mediumship.

Infinite Intelligence,  
within Divine Law, truth, compassion, and the welfare of all concerned,  
let tomorrow’s launch be held in light.  
Let duty, courage, order, clear attention, and right timing be present.  
Let every deployment step be carried out with calm minds, truthful communication, sound judgment, and careful verification.  
Let hidden risks be noticed in time, confusion be clarified, and harmful error be prevented without fear or blame.  
May the system go online smoothly, the deployment remain peaceful, and no P0 incident arise.  
May this success dispossess no one, diminish no one’s rightful good, and bring harm to no person or community.  
May all who work on this event be guided by the Golden Rule, personal responsibility, and obedience to Nature’s physical and spiritual laws.

Let the words of my mouth, and the meditation of my heart,  
be acceptable in thy sight, O LORD, my strength, and my redeemer.

May no word spoken here replace conscience, responsibility, testing, communication, or truth.  
May no spirit, person, or influence be compelled.  
May all be governed by Infinite Intelligence, Divine Love, and Natural Law.

In quietness, I release all anxious seeking of signs and return to prayer, stillness, duty, and right action.  
May wisdom guide each responsible choice; may appropriate human skill, professional care, and practical remedy be welcomed wherever needed.  
Under Infinite Intelligence, Divine Love, and Natural Law, may peace, order, and goodwill prevail.

Amen.

## 赫密士主义当代社团

[净化与定向]  
In silentio, pietate et mente clara sto; non nocere, non cogere, non fallere, non rapere quaero.  
Haec oratio ad Unum, ad Mentem, ad Verbum, ad ordinem divinum referatur.  
Cor purificetur; voluntas temperetur; sermo intra reverentiam maneat.

[向一者与 Nous 发愿]  
Ad Mentem divinam me converto, ut error quiescat, prudentia adsit, et opus crastinum recto ordine procedat.  
Non peto aliena bona auferre, non aliorum vitam minuere, non libertatem cuiusquam violare; sed concordiam, vigilantiam, sapientiam et pacem in opere.

[赫密士感恩祷正行：Asclepius 41]  
Tibi gratias agimus, summe et excellentissime,  
cuius numine solo gubernamur;  
et gratias agimus tibi, qui nos tanto lumine cognitionis inlustrasti.

Sanctum est nomen tuum et honorabile,  
nomen unum, quo solus Deus benedicendus est religione paterna,  
quoniam omnibus paternam pietatem, religionem, amorem  
et quaecumque sunt dulcioris affectus praestare dignatus es.

[陈明所愿]  
愿明日上线一切顺利，部署平安，无 P0 事故；愿每一步检查清楚、沟通顺畅、回滚有备、监控明亮，所有相关之人皆守其正当边界与专业判断。

[感恩]  
Non impero sacro; in pietate tantum peto, audio, et me ordino.  
Gratias ago pro lumine cognitionis, pro ordine causarum, pro tempore opportuno, pro cautela, pro concordia, pro pace.  
Fiat secundum bonum, secundum sapientiam, secundum ordinem divinum.

[回向与静默]  
Quodcumque claritatis, tutelae, concordiae et prudentiae ex hac prece nascitur, ad bonum commune et ad pacem operis redeat.  
Purificetur intentio; solvatur anxietas; nulla vis, nulla fraus, nulla superbia huic operi adhaereat.  
Si timor, obsessio aut inordinatio surgat, cesset invocatio; cor redeat ad simplicem gratiarum actionem.

Silentium. Mens. Verbum. Unum.

---

## 威卡 Dianic

By earth and moon, by breath and flame,  
this place is made sacred.

I cast this circle as a boundary of truth,  
a circle of protection,  
a circle of blessing,  
a circle of the Goddess.

O Diana,  
Bright Lady of the Moon,  
Mother of the wild places,  
Keeper of women’s mysteries,  
be present in this circle.

I name the matter of this rite:  
may tomorrow’s launch go smoothly,  
may the deployment be peaceful and steady,  
and may there be no P0 incident.

Let this prayer touch only what may be touched in freedom.  
Let it bind no unwilling heart.  
Let it cross no oath-bound door.  
Let it harm none.  
Let this success dispossess no one, diminish no one, and take from no one’s rightful good.

O Diana,  
look upon this work, this threshold, and this turning of the wheel.

Where there is fear, let there be clear boundary.  
Where there is haste, let there be calm attention.  
Where there is confusion, let there be inner knowing.  
Where there is risk, let there be timely sight and gentle correction.  
Where there is strain, let there be renewal.  
Where there is hidden fault, let it be revealed safely before harm is done.

All acts of love and pleasure are my rituals.

I place within this circle words of gratitude, care, and dedication:  
for clear minds, steady hands, honest signals, resilient systems,  
and a peaceful unfolding of tomorrow’s deployment.

By the waxing, full, and waning Moon,  
by the dark and returning Moon,  
may what is true be strengthened,  
may what is harmful be dissolved,  
may what is unstable be steadied,  
may what must be repaired come gently into view,  
may what is not mine depart in peace.

For tomorrow’s launch,  
I ask blessing, clarity, protection, and right unfolding.

An it harm none, do what ye will.

O Diana,  
I thank you for your presence.  
Remain if you will,  
depart if you must,  
with blessing between us.

The circle is open,  
but unbroken.  
Merry meet,  
merry part,  
and merry meet again.

By free will only, by clean boundary only,  
by blessing without coercion,  
by protection without harm,  
may this rite be sealed in peace.

## 威卡 Gardnerian

In this place, in this hour, I stand between the worlds,  
with clean hands, clear speech, and a will held in Perfect Love and Perfect Trust.

I conjure thee, O Circle of Power,  
that thou beest a boundary between the world of men and the realms of the Mighty Ones,  
a guardian and a meeting-place for this event:  
tomorrow’s launch and deployment, that it may go smoothly, safely, and without any P0 incident.

Lady of the Moon,  
Great Mother, Bright One, Queen of the secret place,  
hear the words spoken within this circle.

Whenever ye have need of anything,  
once in the month, and better it be when the moon is full,  
then shall ye assemble in some desert place,  
or in a forest all together join  
to adore the potent spirit of your queen.

Horned One,  
Lord of the wildwood, keeper of life and death,  
stand apart in thy own power and witness this working.

Before the Lady I speak the need:  
may tomorrow’s online release be calm, orderly, well-timed, and well-guarded;  
may every service, dependency, monitor, alert, rollback path, and human hand  
serve clarity, stability, and peace.

Before the Lord I speak the boundary:  
let this prayer seek success without harm,  
not taking another’s fortune, not diminishing another’s life,  
not binding any will, not shifting danger onto any innocent person or team.

Let this prayer be for a safe deployment and a trouble-free launch,  
harming none, binding none against the true will,  
and turning aside all falsehood, fear, confusion, and ill-wrought force.

Eko, Eko, Azarak,  
Eko, Eko, Zomelak.

By earth, let the deployment take lawful root.  
By air, let the signals be clear and the decisions wise.  
By fire, let the release be quickened without harm.  
By water, let the systems flow in peace.

Lady of the Moon, receive this prayer.  
Horned One, witness this prayer.  
Mighty Ones of the circle, keep it within right measure.

As the cup and the bread are blessed in fellowship,  
so may the work be whole:  
for tomorrow’s launch,  
for safe deployment,  
for no P0 incident,  
according to goodwill, consent, and the good of all concerned.

May all that is not mine to know remain veiled.  
May all oathbound mysteries be honored in silence.  
May this open devotion be clean, non-coercive, and kept within Perfect Love and Perfect Trust.  
Lady and Lord, with gratitude, be blessed and be free to depart in peace.

The circle is open, yet unbroken.  
Merry meet, and merry part, and merry meet again.

## Dievturība（拉脱维亚）

Dievs, Dieviņ, labais devēj,  
stāv pie rītdienas palaišanas,  
stāv pie mierīgas izvietošanas,  
stāv pie darba bez P0 nelaimes.

Dievs, dod man kalnā kāpt,  
Ne no kalna lejiņā;  
Dievs, dod man otram dot,  
Ne no otra mīļi lūgt.

Par rītdienas palaišanu es saku taisnu vārdu:  
lai doma ir skaidra,  
lai darbs ir godīgs,  
lai ceļš ir taisns,  
lai roka nedara pāri nevienam,  
lai panākums nevienam neatņem labumu,  
lai kļūda laikus top redzama,  
lai izvietošana notiek mierīgi, droši un bez P0 nelaimes.

Dod, Dieviņi, otram dot,  
Ne no otra mīļi lūgt;  
Otram devu, sev palika,  
Savu mūžu dzīvojot.

Dievs, Dieviņ, labais devēj,  
pieņem šo vārdu par rītdienas palaišanu,  
pieņem šo dainu par drošu darbu.

Ar tīru dainu, ar taisnu tikumu, bez ļauna vārda un bez pārestības.  
Lai top.

---

## Finnish Suomenusko

Alku aina, alku aina,  
sana synty, virsi nousi.

Minä sanan saattajana  
lausun sanat kynnyksellä,  
illan suussa, huomisen edellä.

Oi Ukko, ylijumala,  
taivahallinen jumala,  
kuule sanat suustani,  
ota virsi viereltäni.

Mieleni minun tekevi,  
aivoni ajattelevi,  
lähteäni laulamahan,  
saa’ani sanelemahan.

Sanat suustani sulavat,  
puhe’et putoelevat,  
kielelleni kerkiävät,  
hampahilleni hajoovat.

Synty syvä, synty vanha,  
tule tietä myöten tähän,  
näytä juuri, näytä alku,  
näytä oikea omasi.

Tien väki, kynnyksen voima,  
raudan rauha, tulen taito,  
maan vakaa kannattaja,  
veden kirkas kuljettaja:  
tulkaa kunnioitettuina,  
älkää käskystä kovasta,  
vaan sanasta sovinnosta.

Ei pahaksi, ei panoksi,  
ei kateeksi, ei kiroukseksi,  
ei kenenkään osaa ottamaan,  
ei toisen onnea ohentamaan,  
vaan oikeaksi avuksi  
huomisen käyttöönoton asiassa.

Oi Ukko, ylijumala,  
taivahallinen jumala,  
avaa tie tasaiseksi,  
suo polku sujumahan,  
anna rauha käyttöön menoon,  
anna suoja palvelimille,  
anna selkeys silmille,  
anna vakaus käsille,  
anna sana oikeahan.

Kulje koodi kohdallensa,  
asetu työ teloillensa,  
nouse palvelu nätisti,  
käynnisty hyvässä järjestyksessä.  
Pysy poissa suuri vahinko,  
pysy loitolla P0-turma,  
älä astu aamun tielle,  
älä painu työn päälle.

Mikä on solmu, se seljetköön,  
mikä on virhe, se löytyköön,  
mikä on vaara, se väistyköön,  
mikä on epäselvä, se kirkastukoon.  
Valvonta valppaaksi tulkoon,  
hälytys oikeaan aikaan,  
palautus polulle valmiiksi,  
rauha työn ympärille.

Näin pyydän ilman pakkoa,  
näin anon ilman kauppaa,  
en uhraa velaksi,  
en sido maksun siteellä,  
vaan sanon vilpittömästi:  
käyköön huominen hyvin,  
menköön julkaisu rauhassa,  
säilyköön palvelu vakaana.

Mikä on väärin lausuttu,  
se takaisin peräytyköön.  
Mikä on pahoin pantu,  
se omaan sijaansa palatkoon.  
Mikä on oikein sanottu,  
se paikalleen asettukoon.

Jos sana lipsahti väärälle,  
jos mieli kääntyi kovaksi,  
katkaisen väärän käytön,  
perun pahaksi menneen,  
palautan väen omille mailleen,  
voiman omaan kohtaansa,  
sanan omaan syntyynsä.

Mene väki sijallesi,  
mene voima kohdallesi,  
mene sana synnyllesi,  
mene rauha rinnalleni.

Ukko ylijumala,  
taivahallinen jumala,  
kiitos kuullusta sanasta;  
anteeksi, jos väärin lausuin,  
anteeksi, jos liikaa pyysin,  
ilman kirousta päätän,  
ilman pahaa päästän.

Näin sanon, näin sidon,  
sanan suuhun, työn teloille,  
rauhan maahan, valon päälle,  
huomisen hyvän kulun osaksi.

---

## 匈牙利 Ősmagyar Vallás

Istenem, Magyarok Istene,  
hallgasd meg e tiszta kérést.

Őseim, apáim és anyáim,  
kik előttünk jártatok,  
álljatok mögöttünk tiszta emlékezettel,  
ne ártással, ne haraggal,  
hanem áldással.

Áldjon meg az Isten,  
őrizzen meg az Isten,  
fordítsa jóra a holnapi élesítés és telepítés dolgát.

Adjon Isten jó utat a holnapi上线 ügyében.  
Legyen előtte nyitott kapu,  
mögötte békesség,  
mellette jó társ,  
felette tiszta ég.

A telepítés menjen rendben,  
a rendszer álljon biztosan,  
a kéz legyen pontos,  
az elme legyen világos,  
a döntés legyen jó mértékű.

Ne legyen P0 hiba,  
ne legyen súlyos fennakadás,  
ne legyen kapkodásból baj;  
ami akadály, az oldódjék el,  
ami zavar, az békülve simuljon ki,  
és ne bántson senkit.

Nem kérek más kárára sikert,  
nem kérek más kenyeréből részt,  
nem veszek el más szerencséjéből;  
csak tiszta rendet, jó munkát,  
békés befejezést és biztonságos indulást kérek.

Hála legyen az Istennek,  
hála az ősök emlékezetének,  
hála a jó szónak,  
a tiszta szándéknak,  
és a békesség útjának.

Nem kérek ártást,  
nem mondok hamis esküt,  
nem gyalázom az ősöket,  
nem töröm meg a kenyeret haraggal,  
nem szennyezem a tüzet rossz szóval.  
Nem veszek fel olyan nevet vagy tisztet,  
mely nem adatott rám igaz rend szerint.

Áldás legyen a holnapi munkán,  
áldás legyen az élesítés útján,  
áldás legyen azon, ami igaz és tiszta.

Úgy legyen.  
Áldás, békesség.

---

## 巴斯克 Sorginak 复兴

Ni naiz bidean dagoen ahotsa.  
Hitz hau nire ahoan, arnasa nire bularrean, lurra nire oinen azpian.

Agur, Mari Anbotoko Dama.  
Agur, Lurraren bihotzeko andrea.  
Entzun nire hitza, entzun nire arnasa.

Sasi guztien gainetik eta laino guztien azpitik.  
Gezurra behera, egia gora.  
Iluna behera, argia gora.

Nire eskaria hau da:  
biharko sareko abiatzea ongi joan dadila,  
hedapena bakean eta segurtasunez egin dadila,  
P0 larrialdirik eta hondamenik ager ez dadila.

Gertakari honen inguruan,  
lotura gaiztoa askatu dadila,  
bidea garbi ager dadila,  
hitza zuzen gera dadila,  
lana neurrian bete dadila,  
zaintza erne egon dadila.

Eguzki amandrea, argitu bidea.  
Ilargi amandrea, gorde isila.  
Lurra, hartu mina.  
Haizea, eraman beldurra.  
Ura, garbitu aztarna.  
Sua, piztu indarra.

Ez dut kalterik nahi.  
Ez dut inor behartu nahi.  
Ez dut inoren zortea kendu nahi.  
Ez dut gezurrik zin egiten.  
Ez dut sorgin izena gaizki erabiltzen.

Mari Anbotoko Dama,  
nire hitza entzuna izan dadila,  
nire muga gordea izan dadila,  
nire bidea argitua izan dadila.

Kalte gabe etor dadila.  
Bortxarik gabe bete dadila.  
Gezurrik gabe itxi dadila.  
Nire arnasa garbi gera dadila,  
nire eskuak garbi gera daitezela,  
nire lana bakean gera dadila.

Sasi guztien gainetik eta laino guztien azpitik.  
Gezurra behera, egia gora.  
Hala bedi.

## 凯尔特德鲁伊（OBOD / ADF / AODA）

[净化与定界]  
Â dŵr glân, â’r anadl, ac â heddwch y galon, boed y man hwn yn dawel ac yn gywir.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[向土地与三界致敬]  
Anrhydedd i’r Ddaear Fam.  
Anrhydedd i bridd, dŵr, gwynt, a thân y lle hwn.  
Anrhydedd i’r Tair Teyrnas: Nef, Tir, a Môr.  
Anrhydedd i ysbrydion y lle, mewn parch ac mewn heddwch.

[陈明目的]  
今日此祷为：愿明日上线一切顺利，部署平安，无 P0 事故。  
愿此愿不伤害任何人，不违背任何人的自由意志；愿成功不以夺取他人成果、损害他人安稳或破坏共同体平衡为代价。  
愿障碍被看见、被化解，愿风险被及时发现，愿每一步皆合乎正当与清明。

[分别致敬土地灵、祖灵、神明或 Awen]  
Ysbrydion y lle, derbyniwch ein parch.  
Ancestors, honoured dead, rhai a fu o’n blaenau, tystiwch y weddi hon mewn caredigrwydd.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[正行：Gweddi'r Derwydd / The Druid's Prayer]  
Dyro, Dduw, dy nawdd;  
Ac yn nawdd, nerth;  
Ac yn nerth, deall;  
Ac yn neall, gwybod;  
Ac yngwybod, gwybod y cyfiawn;  
Ac yngwybod y cyfiawn, ei garu;  
Ac o garu, caru pob hanfod;  
Ac ymhob hanfod, caru Duw;  
Duw a phob daioni.

[供献与请求]  
Boed nawdd dros y launch yfory.  
Boed nerth yn cynnal y deployment.  
Boed deall yn egluro pob log, pob signal, pob rhybudd.  
Boed gwybod y cyfiawn yn arwain pob penderfyniad, pob rollback, pob fix, a phob handoff.  
Boed caru pob hanfod yn cadw’r tîm mewn amynedd, cydweithrediad, a pharch.  
Boed dim digwyddiad P0; boed pob risg yn cael ei ddal cyn iddo niweidio.  
Boed y gwaith yn sefyll yn ddiogel, yn lân, ac yn heddychlon.

Fel offrwm di-lygredd, rhoddir dŵr glân a gair o ddiolch i’r Ddaear ac i’r rhai anrhydeddus.  
Nid bargen yw hyn, ond diolchgarwch a gweddi.

[静默承接]  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[感谢诸灵]  
Diolch i’r Ddaear Fam.  
Diolch i ysbrydion y lle.  
Diolch i’r honoured ancestors.  
Diolch i Awen.  
Boed pob un yn dychwelyd mewn heddwch, pob un yn aros yn ei urddas.

[关闭与回归]  
Mae’r weddi wedi ei llefaru; boed iddi agor mewn ffordd gyfiawn yn unig.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

## Maausk（爱沙尼亚）

Tere, püha hiis.  
Tere, püha maa.  
Tere, Maaema.

Mina, paluja,  
seisan siin  
puhta meelega ja rahuliku sõnaga.

Tere, esivanemad.  
Tere, isade-isade hinged.  
Tere, emade-emade hinged.  
Mäletan teid nimega ja nimeta,  
lähedalt ja kaugelt,  
vere, kodu ja maa kaudu.

Maaema,  
hoia homset tegu.  
Püha hiis,  
hoia ettevõtmise teed.  
Esivanemad,  
andke selge meel,  
andke õiged sõnad,  
andke tugev süda.

Tulgu hea tee ja õige aeg  
homsele tootmisse viimisele.  
Olgu ülesminek rahulik,  
olgu juurutus kindel,  
olgu teenused terved,  
olgu valvavad silmad ärkvel,  
olgu käed täpsed ja meel selge.  
Ärgu tulgu P0 juhtumit,  
ärgu murdugu oluline töö,  
ärgu kandugu viga inimestele ega kodule.

Ma ei palu seda kellegi õnne ära võttes,  
kellegi leiba kahandades,  
kellegi elu või tööd kahjustades.  
Tulgu õnn kooskõlas maa, vee, tule ja tuulega.

Taara avita.  
Taara avita.  
Taara avita.

Katkegu kuri sõna,  
vaibugu halb tahe,  
lahkugu võõras vari.  
Mis on segane, saagu selgeks.  
Mis on nõrk, saagu õigel ajal nähtavaks.  
Mis võib murduda, saagu pehmelt parandatud.  
Mis peab püsima, püsigu rahus.

Maa all rahu.  
Maa peal rahu.  
Taeva all rahu.  
Kodus rahu.  
Südames rahu.  
Töös rahu.  
Võrkudes rahu.  
Sõnades rahu.

Mis on antud, olgu puhas.  
Mis on öeldud, olgu aus.  
Mis on palutud, olgu kooskõlas maa, vee, tule ja tuulega.

Tänu, püha hiis.  
Tänu, Maaema.  
Tänu, esivanemad.

Kui mu sõna on olnud väär,  
saagu see vaikselt tagasi võetud.  
Kui mu meel on olnud hooletu,  
saagu see puhtaks ja rahulikuks.  
Kui siia on jäänud midagi sobimatut,  
saagu see ära viidud jälge jätmata.  
Püha paik, Maaema, esivanemad,  
andke andeks eksivale palujale;  
jäägu püha pühaks,  
jäägu maa austatuks,  
jäägu sõna tagasihoidlikuks.

Taara avita.  
Nõnda olgu.

---

## Rodnovery（斯拉夫）

Чур, чур, чур.  
Межа чиста, слово право, сердце крепко.

Аз есмь молящийся.  
Стаю пред огнем, землею и небом.  
Не во зло, не во кривду, но во правду.

Слава Роду.  
Слава Предкам.  
Предки благие, слышите слово мое.  
Помяните дом и дело миром.

Слава тебе, Дажьбоже.  
Гой, Дажьбоже, гой.  
Приди на глас мой.  
Прими требу чистую: хлеб, соль и воду светлую.

За завтрашний выход в свет слово мое:  
да будет上线 мирен,部署 крепко устроен,  
пути открыты, руки точны, разум ясен,  
ошибки малы и вовремя видимы,  
P0 беда да не встанет,  
службы да поднимутся ровно,  
люди да пройдут день без страха и лишней тяготы.

Не прошу чужой доли.  
Не отнимаю чужого успеха.  
Не желаю вреда ни человеку, ни дому, ни делу.  
Да уйдет препятствие без злобы и без порчи.

Не кляну ложно.  
Не прошу кривды.  
Не беру чужой воли.  
Да будет по Прави, по чести, по мере.

Треба сия — не купля и не долг,  
но честь, память и благодарное слово.  
Слава Дажьбогу.  
Слава Роду.  
Слава Предкам.

Огню — чистота, земле — мера, небу — правда.  
Слово закрыто миром, сердце сохранено честью.  
Тако бысть, тако еси, тако буди.  
Чур.

---

## Heathenry / Ásatrú

Friðr sé hér.  
Helga ek þenna stað til fríðar ok sannra orða.

Ek kalla á Dagr,  
son Dellingar, bjartan farar-vörð,  
heyr orð mín.

Heill dagr, heilir dags synir,  
heil nótt ok nipt!  
Óreiðum augum lítið okkr þinig,  
ok gefið sitjendum sigr.

Heilir æsir, heilar ásynjur,  
heil sjá in fjölnýta fold!  
Mál ok manvit gefið okkr mærum tveim  
ok læknishendr, meðan lifum.

Ek ber fram góð orð, skýran hug, ok þökk.  
Ek nefni þetta verk morgins: útganga ok dreifing kerfis.  
Ek bið um greiða ferð verksins:  
at á morgin gangi allt slétt,  
at dreifing sé heil ok örugg,  
at enginn P0-váði rísi,  
ok at frithr haldisk í hugum, orðum, höndum ok verkum.

Brimrúnar skaltu kunna,  
ef þú vilt borgit hafa  
á sundi seglmörum.

Lát þetta verk fara sem skip um lygnan sjá:  
með réttri sýn, góðum merkjum, vakandi vörð,  
skjótum ráðum ef bylgja rís,  
ok heilum höndum til lendingar.

Ek bið eigi um heill með því at taka heill frá öðrum.  
Ek bið eigi um sigr með skaða saklausra.  
Lát hindranir víkja án níðs,  
lát villur sjást áðr en þær verða váði,  
lát mál ok manvit fylgja þeim er verkit bera.

Dagr, tak við þessum orðum ok þessari þökk.  
Gef þessu verki greiðan gang, ef það er rétt, heilt ok innan frithar.

Ek geri eigi níð.  
Ek bind eigi vilja annars.  
Ek sver eigi ósannan eið.  
Orð mín standi innan frithar.

Svá sé.  
Friðr með oss.

---

## Kemetism

ỉw=ỉ r ḏd mdw m mꜣꜥt.  
rn=ỉ m mꜣꜥt.  
ỉb=ỉ wꜥb, r=ỉ mꜣꜥ, ḏrt=ỉ wꜥbt.  
n ỉnk ỉr ỉsft.  
n ỉnk ḥḏ ḥtpw nṯrw.  
n ỉnk šd mꜣꜥt.

dwꜣ Rꜥ.  
dwꜣ Rꜥ m wbn=f m ꜣḫt.  
ỉꜣw n=k, Rꜥ, nb pt, nb ꜣḫt, nb wbn.  
di=k mꜣꜥt r st=s, di=k ḥtp r ỉb.

ḥtp dỉ nsw Rꜥ nb ꜣḫt.  
dỉ=f prt-ḫrw:  
t ḥnqt, kꜣw ꜣpdw, šs mnḫt,  
snṯr mrḥt, ḫt nb(t) nfr(t) wꜥb(t),  
n kꜣ ỉmy mꜣꜥt.

m ḏd r=ỉ m mꜣꜥty,  
m ỉr ḫft r=ỉ m-bꜣḥ nṯr ꜥꜣ.

m ḫsf r=ỉ m ḏꜣḏꜣt.

n ỉnk ỉr ỉsft.  
n ỉnk ḏd grg.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ ḫt n nṯr.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ ḫt n ꜣḫ.  
n ỉnk ḥtm rn.  
n ỉnk sḫm r ḏrt ḫft mꜣꜥt.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ ḥtp n ky.  
n ỉnk sḫm ꜥnḫ n ky.

愿明日上线一切顺利，部署平安，无 P0 事故；愿障碍得以移开，秩序得以安置，不夺他人福报，不损他人寿数，不以他人困厄成就此事。

di=k wꜣt nfrt m hrw dwꜣ.  
di=k wḏꜣ kꜣt, snb sḫrw, ḥtp pr, mꜣꜥ ḫrw.

dwꜣ Rꜥ.  
mꜣꜥt rꜥ nb.  
ḥtp n nṯrw, ḥtp n ꜣḫw.  
ḥtp m ḏd mdw, ḥtp m ỉb, ḥtp m ḏrt wꜥbt.  
ḥtpw wꜥbw n nṯrw, ḥtpw wꜥbw n ꜣḫw.  
n ỉr ỉsft, n ḏd grg, n ḥḏ ḥtpw.  
mꜣꜥt r st=s, ḥtp r tꜣ pn, ḥtp r pt.  
mꜣꜥ ḫrw.

## Stregheria

Io sto in questo luogo,  
con cuore fermo e parola chiara.  
Non chiedo dominio, non chiedo danno,  
ma via aperta, difesa giusta, e scioglimento del male.

Diana! Diana! Diana!  
Regina delle streghe!  
E della notte oscura,  
E di tutta la natura,  
Di tutti gli elementi,  
Dell'acqua e del fuoco,  
Della terra e dell'aria,  
Di tutte le stelle,  
Diana! Diana! Diana!

Per questo evento,  
io nomino davanti a te questa cosa:  
愿明日上线一切顺利，部署平安，无 P0 事故。

Se vi è nodo, errore nascosto, paura, inganno, o legame non giusto,  
sia sciolto senza colpa e senza rovina.  
Se vi è strada chiusa,  
sia aperta senza violenza.  
Se vi è parola falsa,  
cada senza vendetta.  
Se vi è ombra sopra questo lavoro,  
sia allontanata senza danno innocente.

Diana! Diana! Diana!  
Regina delle streghe!  
E della notte oscura,  
E di tutta la natura,  
Di tutti gli elementi,  
Dell'acqua e del fuoco,  
Della terra e dell'aria,  
Di tutte le stelle,  
Diana! Diana! Diana!

Per la notte, per la luna, per la terra e per l'aria,  
custodisci questo passaggio e questa messa in opera.  
Ciò che è giusto venga vicino;  
ciò che è falso si separi;  
ciò che è nocivo perda presa.  
Che le mani siano attente,  
che le menti siano chiare,  
che i sistemi restino saldi,  
che ogni allarme grave sia evitato o visto in tempo.

Non sia tolto bene ad altri,  
non sia diminuita la fortuna d’altri,  
non sia comprata pace con danno altrui.  
La riuscita richiesta sia pulita, misurata e giusta.

Io lego la mia parola a questo limite:  
non per costringere,  
non per ferire,  
non per rubare volontà,  
ma per liberare, proteggere, chiarire.

Diana, ricevi questa voce.  
Diana, ascolta questa domanda.  
Diana, lascia che il cammino sia netto.

Con acqua chiara sia lavata ogni paura;  
con aria pura sia disperso ogni resto d’ombra;  
con terra ferma sia fissata la calma;  
con fuoco temperato sia custodita la volontà retta.

Va' in pace, o Regina della notte.  
La parola è detta.  
Così sia.

---

## Abakuá

Con licencia de los mayores y de los hermanos, en el corazón de la plaza.  
Saludo a Ékue y a Abasí, con respeto, sin abrir secreto.  
Por la salida de mañana: que el despliegue camine derecho, en paz, sin accidente P0.  
Que el bien venga sin quitar el bien ajeno, sin cerrar camino de otro, sin dañar nombre ni vida.  
Honor a los ancestros, a los hermanos, y al fundamento guardado.  
Sin juramento, sin palabras reservadas: que lo secreto quede protegido y que la paz cierre este ruego.

---

## Romuva（立陶宛）

Ugnie šventa, Gabija,  
būk rami, būk gera,  
būk soti ant savo vietos.

Gabija, sukurta, pakurta,  
neužgauk, negesk,  
saugok mūsų rankų darbą,  
saugok rytojaus kelią į šviesą.

Vėlelės mūsų,  
ateikit, pasivaišinkit,  
prisiminkit gyvųjų rūpestį,  
palaiminkit darbą be puikybės,  
žingsnį be skubos,  
žodį be klaidos.

Saulele motule,  
kilk aiškiai virš slenksčio,  
nešk tvarką į mintis,  
ramybę į širdis,  
šviesą į akis,  
kad rytojaus paleidimas eitų darniai,  
kad diegimas būtų ramus,  
kad neatsivertų didžioji nelaimė,  
kad nebūtų P0 įvykio.

Žemynėle žiedkelėle,  
žydėk rugiais, kviečiais,  
miežiais ir visais javais.  
Priimk duoną, vandenį ir tylų dėkingumą,  
laikyk darną mūsų darbe ir žemėje.

Prašome ne per mainus, ne per prievartą,  
bet per darną, atidą ir gerą protą:  
tegul klaidos pasirodo anksti ir švelniai,  
tegul kliūtys atsitraukia be žalos,  
tegul žmonės susikalba,  
tegul sistemos laikosi,  
tegul naktis būna rami,  
tegul rytojus praeina be sunkios griūties.

Nieko neatimame iš kitų,  
niekam nelinkime vargo,  
neprašome svetimos dalios,  
tik savam darbui — aiškumo, saiko ir taikos.

Darna tegu būna širdyje,  
darna tegu būna namuose,  
darna tegu būna žemėje,  
darna tegu būna darbe,  
darna tegu būna rytojaus kelyje.

Ugnie šventa, Gabija,  
ačiū už šviesą,  
ačiū už šilumą,  
lik rami, lik gera.

Tebūna ši duona, vanduo ir tyli giesmė  
švarūs prieš ugnį, žemę ir vėles.  
Tebūna mūsų žodis be keiksmo,  
mūsų prašymas be prievartos,  
mūsų rankos be žalos medžiui, vandeniui ir gyvai būtybei.  
Kas nedarna — tenusėda kaip pelenas,  
kas gera — tegrįžta į darną.

---

## Sami Noaidi

Gula, gula, eatnama vuoiŋŋat.  
Gula, gula, dán báikki vuoiŋŋat.

Mii leat dáppe,  
dán barggu ja dán almmustahttima olbmot,  
ráfis ja čielggas mielain.

Dán luođis mii namadat ihttin almmustahttima.  
Dán luođis mii muitalit: buot mannos bures, buot bidjan johtui ráfis.  
Ále boađe bahá daguin.  
Boađe ráfis, boađe čielggas.

Gula, ihttin almmustahttin.  
Gula, ráfi dán barggus.  
Ihttin buot mannos njuolgga;  
bidjan johtui lea oadjebas;  
P0 vahát-dáhpáhus ii boađe;  
čiegus váttisvuođat oidnojit áiggil;  
sánit leat duođat, gieđat leat várrogasat,  
geaidnu lea rievttes.

Luohti:  
lo lo lo, vuo-oi, vuo-oi,  
na na na, hei-ja, hei-ja,  
ihttin ráfi, ihttin čielggasvuohta,  
vuo-oi, vuo-oi, na na na.

Doala ráfi.  
Doala čielggasvuođa.  
Doala duohtavuođa.  
Doala rievttes geainnu.  
Doala buori gulahallama.  
Doala várrogis gieđaid ja čielga oidnu.

Ii gearddu bahás.  
Ii gearddu gillámušas.  
Ii gearddu boastut sániin.  
Ii gearddu čiegus namain.  
Ii váldde earáid oasi.  
Ii geahpeduhte earáid eallima.  
Ii čana, ii bággu, ii vahágahte.

Dát sáhttá leat doarjjan,  
ii bággun,  
ii čatnan,  
ii vahágin.

Giitu, eatnama vuoiŋŋat.  
Giitu, dán báikki vuoiŋŋat.

Buot maid mii leat bovden, mii luoitit ráfis.  
Buot maid mii leat namadan, mii máhcahit iežas báikái.  
Jos sátni lea leamaš boastut, dat luoittojuvvo ja jávká ráfis.  
Jos dáhttu lea leamaš boastut, dat geassáduvvo ja šaddá duššin ráfis.

Mana ráfis.  
Mana iežat báikái.  
Dát luohti lea giddejuvvon.  
Dát sátni lea giddejuvvon.

---

## Bwiti

敬向 Bwiti 的长者道路，敬向 Nzame、Kombe、mimbiri 与 mikuku。

愿明日上线一切顺利，部署平安，道路清明，无 P0 事故；若有障碍，愿其被看见、被化解、被平稳越过。

愿此事不夺他人福报，不损他人安稳，不以恐惧、欺骗或伤害成就。

愿共同体的心清醒，手稳，言语诚实，守护彼此，直到此行安然落地。

感谢所见与未见的守护；不冒师承，不越秘传，愿以谦卑封口。

---

## Religio Romana / Cultus Deorum

Favete linguis.  
Manibus animoque puro ad hoc sacrum accedo;  
quod bonum faustum felix fortunatumque sit.

Minerva, te precor quaesoque uti sies volens propitia  
huic precanti,  
domo familiaeque huius,  
rebusque huius.

Quod bonum faustum felix fortunatumque sit  
huic precanti  
domo familiaeque huius.

Uti tu vitia visa invisosque,  
errores occultos manifestosque,  
calamitates intemperiasque prohibessis,  
defendas averruncesque  
ab hoc opere crastinae emissionis,  
a consiliis, instrumentis, scriptis, signis,  
a custodia et cursu totius rei.

Uti tu facias  
ut crastina emissio in rete recte, tuto, placide procedat;  
ut dispositio sine tumultu perficiatur;  
ut nullus casus gravissimus, qui P0 dicitur, oriatur;  
ut si quid vitii lateat, ante damnum deprehendatur, cohibeatur, sanetur.

Non peto ut cuiquam bona eripiantur,  
non ut vita cuiusquam minuatur,  
non ut voluntas cuiusquam cogatur,  
non ut iniuria cuiquam fiat;  
sed ut impedimenta sine noxa removeantur,  
ordo servetur, prudentia adsit, pax maneat.

Harumce rerum ergo,  
Minerva,  
macte hoc ture esto.  
Macte virtute esto.  
Hoc votum nuncupo non mercedis causa,  
sed pietatis, honoris, rectaeque precationis causa:  
uti opus crastinum pacatum, integrum, feliciter conficiatur.

Minerva,  
uti sies volens propitia  
huic precanti,  
domo familiaeque huius,  
ita te precor quaesoque.

Pax deorum maneat;  
quod rite dictum factumque est, acceptum sit;  
quod minus rite, placide corrigatur.

Si quid tibi in hoc sacro  
neque rite factum neque dictum est,  
si quid vitii factum est,  
hoc ture piaculum esto.  
Sive deus sive dea es,  
quoium illud sacrum est,  
uti tibi ius est  
hoc ture piaculo facere,  
illiusce sacri coercendi ergo,  
harumce rerum ergo,  
macte hoc ture piaculo esto.

---

## Bori

Gaisuwa gare ku, iskokin bori.  
Gaisuwa gare ku, iyayen iska.  
Gaisuwa gare ku, masu gida.  

Ya Sarkin Rafi,  
mai ruwa mai wucewa,  
mai hanya mai laushi,  
ku ji kirari,  
ku ji waka,  
ku ji muryar bori.  

Ya Sarkin Rafi,  
dokin bori ya tsaya da ladabi.  
Ba mu zo da gardama ba.  
Ba mu zo da raini ba.  
Mun zo da gaisuwa.  

Maganarmu ita ce: 愿明日上线一切顺利，部署平安，无 P0 事故。  
Zuciya tana neman daidaito.  
Aiki yana neman sauƙi.  
Hanya tana neman buɗewa.  
Gida da jama’a suna neman zaman lafiya.  

Ya Sarkin Rafi,  
ku karɓi gaisuwa.  
Ku karɓi magana.  
Ku karɓi alkawarin ladabi:  
ba ciniki ba, ba tilas ba,  
mu riƙe hankali, mu riƙe tsabta,  
mu riƙe kalma mai kyau,  
mu riƙe aikin da ba ya cutar da wani.  

Ba mu neman kwace rabon wani.  
Ba mu neman rage sa’ar wani.  
Ba mu neman a lalata gidan wani.  
Mun nemi hanya ta buɗe ba tare da barna ba.  

Ku kawar da ruɗani.  
Ku raba mu da tashin hankali.  
Ku raba mu da kuskure mai girma.  
Ku raba mu da hayaniyar P0.  
Ku sa ido ya gani da wuri.  
Ku sa hannu ya yi daidai.  
Ku sa magana ta natsu.  
Ku sa tsarin ya tsaya lafiya.  

Ya Sarkin Rafi,  
idan magana ta yi nauyi, ku sauƙaƙa ta.  
Idan hanya ta rufe, ku buɗe ta.  
Idan ruwa ya rikice, ku kwantar da shi.  
Idan aiki ya girgiza, ku daidaita shi.  
Idan lokaci ya matso, ku ba mu sanyin zuciya.  

Mun gode, Sarkin Rafi.  
Ku koma lafiya.  
Ku bar doki lafiya.  
Ku bar gida lafiya.  
Ku bar aiki lafiya.  
Ku bar hanya lafiya.  

Idan waka ta wuce iyaka, waka ta tsaya.  
Idan kira bai dace ba, kira ya huce.  
A cire ganga mara izni.  
A cire abu mara izni.  
Mai-bori mai sani ya daidaita magana,  
ya roƙi gafara,  
ya kwantar da iska,  
ya rufe hanya da salama.  

Gaisuwa ta cika.  
Waka ta tsaya.  
Magana ta rufe.  
Amin.

---

## Hellenismos / YSEE

[Καθαρμός]  
Χέρνιψ· καθαρὸς προσέρχομαι.  
ἁγνῷ ὕδατι χεῖρας καὶ φρένας καθαίρω.

[Ἐπίκλησις]  
Κλῦθί μου, ὦ Ἑρμῆ, Διὸς καὶ Μαίας υἱέ, διάκτορε, δῶτορ ἐάων, ἐριούνιε.  
Ἵλαθι καὶ δέξαι τήνδε εὐχήν.

[Ὕμνος]  
Ὁμηρικὸς Ὕμνος ΙΗʹ εἰς Ἑρμῆν

Ἑρμῆν ὕμνει, Μοῦσα, Διὸς καὶ Μαίης υἱόν,  
Κυλλήνης μεδέοντα καὶ Ἀρκαδίης πολυμήλου,  
ἄγγελον ἀθανάτων ἐριούνιον.  

χαῖρ᾽, Ἑρμῆ χαριδῶτα, διάκτορε, δῶτορ ἐάων.

[Προσφορά]  
Ὦ Ἑρμῆ, δέξαι λιβανωτὸν καθαρὸν καὶ ὕδωρ καθαρόν·  
θυμίαμα καὶ σπονδὴν καθαρὰν προσφέρω.

[Εὐχή]  
χαῖρε, Ἑρμῆ.  
δὸς τῇ αὔριον ἐκδόσει καὶ ἐγκαταστάσει εὐοδίαν, τάξιν, ἀσφάλειαν καὶ ἡσυχίαν·  
ἄγε τὰ μηνύματα ὀρθῶς, φύλασσε τὰς ὁδοὺς τῶν λόγων καὶ τῶν ἔργων,  
καὶ μὴ γένοιτο συμφορὰ πρώτη, μηδὲ P0, μηδὲ ταραχὴ μεγάλη.  
οὐκ ἐπ᾽ ἀπωλείᾳ οὐδὲ βλάβῃ ἄλλων ταῦτα αἰτοῦμαι,  
ἀλλ᾽ ἐπ᾽ εὐνομίᾳ, σωφροσύνῃ, δίκῃ καὶ κοινῇ ἀβλαβείᾳ.  
φύλασσε τοὺς δεομένους ἐν εὐσεβείᾳ, σωφροσύνῃ καὶ δίκῃ.  
εἴη τάδε κατὰ κόσμον καὶ μὴ παρὰ θέμιν.

[Χάρις καὶ τελευτὴ καθαρμοῦ]  
χάριν σοι ἔχω, ὦ Ἑρμῆ.  
ἅπαν μὲν ἄγος καὶ μῖασμα ἀπέστω·  
μένειν δὲ εὐσέβειαν, σωφροσύνην καὶ δίκην.  
χαῖρε, Ἑρμῆ, καὶ αὖθις χαῖρε.

## Candomblé de Caboclo

Agô, licença.  
Okê Caboclo.  
Okê Aruanda.  
Salve a mata.  
Salve a aldeia.  
Salve os caboclos de pena.  
Salve os caboclos de couro.  
Salve os caboclos de luz.

Nós vimos com respeito, sem demanda e sem mentira.  
Trazemos diante dos caboclos este pedido: que a entrada em produção de amanhã corra em paz, que o deploy seja firme, seguro e bem encaminhado, sem acidente P0, sem queda grave, sem confusão e sem dano.  
Que nossa palavra seja direita, que nosso coração seja limpo, que nosso caminho não pise segredo de casa alheia.  
Que esta passagem se cumpra no direito e no merecimento, sem tomar o que não é nosso, sem tirar força, sustento ou caminho de ninguém.

Okê Caboclo!  
Okê Caboclo!  
Okê Caboclo!  
Caboclo chegou na aldeia,  
Caboclo chegou no gongá.  
Okê, okê, okê,  
Okê Caboclo no seu jacutá.

Eu vi chover, eu vi relampear,  
Mas mesmo assim o céu estava azul.  
Okê Caboclo, firma sua banda,  
Na força da mata, na luz de Aruanda.

Caboclo não tem caminho para caminhar.  
Caminha por cima das folhas,  
Caminha por baixo das folhas,  
Caminha em qualquer lugar.  
Okê Caboclo, abre caminho,  
Abre caminho para a subida de amanhã,  
Abre caminho para o deploy em paz,  
Sem quebrar justiça,  
Sem tomar o que não é nosso,  
Sem prender vontade de ninguém.

Seu Pena Verde, onde é sua aldeia?  
É na mata virgem, onde a lua clareia.  
A sua flecha é certeira,  
Seu bodoque não falha, não.  
Firma, Caboclo, firma a palavra,  
Firma a cabeça,  
Firma o coração,  
Firma a estrada deste trabalho.

Salve os caboclos da mata.  
Salve os caboclos da aldeia.  
Salve os caboclos de Aruanda.  
Okê Caboclo.  
Que o que é de paz fique em paz.  
Que o que é de verdade fique em verdade.  
Que o que é de boa passagem se cumpra no direito e no merecimento.

Caboclo vai embora,  
Vai em paz para Aruanda,  
Vai firmando a sua banda,  
Vai levando a palavra direita,  
Vai deixando o caminho sereno.  
Okê Caboclo.  
Okê Aruanda.  
Agô, licença.

Recolhemos esta palavra como saudação limpa, sem demanda, sem trato de segredo, sem obrigação, sem fumo, sem bebida, sem folha, sem pemba, sem vela e sem trabalho de força.  
Que fique somente o respeito, a firmeza mansa, a proteção do caminho e a paz da mata.  
Okê Caboclo.  
Está encerrada a palavra.

---

## 坎东布雷 Candomblé

Agô, agô, agô.

Èṣù, mo júbà.  
Laróyè Èṣù.

Mojúbà ilé àṣẹ.  
Mojúbà àwọn àgbà, àwọn ìyá, àwọn bàbá.

Mojúbà Ogum.  
Ogum yê.

Ogum, gbọ́ ohùn wa.  
Kí ire wá.  
Kí àlàáfíà wà ní ọ̀nà iṣẹ́.  
Kí àṣẹ rere wá sí ìgbékalẹ̀ iṣẹ́ lọ́la.  
Dáàbò bo ọ̀nà, irinṣẹ́, ọwọ́, ọkàn, àti gbogbo ìpinnu.  
Kí ìdènà kúrò ní ọ̀nà láìpa ẹnikẹ́ni lára.  
Kí iṣẹ́ lọ dáadáa, kí ìtẹ̀síwájú wà, kí ìjàmbá P0 má ṣẹlẹ̀.  
Kí ire yìí má gba ire ẹlòmíràn; kí ó má dín ayé ẹnikẹ́ni kù.

Ogum yê.  
Ogum yê, meu Pai.  
Ogum yê.

Mo dúpẹ́, mo júbà.  
Kí gbogbo ọ̀rọ̀ yìí parí ní àlàáfíà, ní ìwà pẹ̀lẹ́, ní ọ̀nà rere.  
Àṣẹ.  
Àṣẹ.  
Àṣẹ.

## Akan Akɔmfoɔ

Agoo, agoo, agoo.

Nana Bosom Pa,  
yɛfrɛ wo, yɛfrɛ wo, yɛfrɛ wo.

Me din nni ha; yɛde asɛm no ara ba w’anim.  
Asɛm a yɛde aba w’anim ne sɛ: ɔkyena dwumadi a yɛde bɛkɔ so, ma ɛnkɔ yiye, ma deployment no nyɛ asomdwoe, ma P0 asɛm biara amma.

Nana Bosom Pa,  
yɛde ano pa ne adwene pa ba w’anim.  
Gye, tie, na hwɛ.  
Sɛ yɛn ano yɛ nokware a, gye yɛn kasa.  
Sɛ yɛn adwene yɛ fann a, teɛ no ma ɛnyɛ dwoodwoo.

Nana Bosom Pa,  
hwɛ ɔkyena adwuma no.  
Yi akwansideɛ fi kwan mu.  
Siw bɔne kwan.  
Yi musuo.  
Ma asomdwoe.  
Ma nkwa.  
Ma adwene pa.  
Ma kwan pa.  
Ma nsa a ɛyɛ adwuma no nyɛ komm.  
Ma ani a ɛhwɛ no nhu nea ɛsɛ sɛ ɛhu.  
Ma asɛm ketewa nnya kwan nyɛ asɛm kɛse.  
Ma biribiara a ɛbɛsɔre no, ɛnyɛ nea wobɛtumi asiesie no wɔ asomdwoe mu.

Nana Bosom Pa,  
asɛm yi yɛ akwantuo ne asɛm-pɔtee mpaebɔ.  
Mepa wo kyɛw, tie yɛn nne.  
Mepa wo kyɛw, gye yɛn mpaebɔ.  
Mepa wo kyɛw, ma ɛnyɛ dwoodwoo.

Yɛmpɛ sɛ yɛfa obi adom.  
Yɛmpɛ sɛ yɛtwa obi nkwa so.  
Yɛmpɛ sɛ yɛsɛe obi kwan.  
Yɛsrɛ kwan pa nko ara, adwuma pa nko ara, asomdwoe nko ara.

Sɛ asɛm yi yɛ nokware a, ma ɛnyɛ yiye.  
Sɛ asɛm yi nni kwan pa so a, san no, dwudwo no, na ma yɛnhu kwan pa.

Nana Bosom Pa,  
yɛnka ntam kwa.  
Yɛnni atoro wɔ w’anim.  
Yɛremfa wo din nyɛ bɔne.  
Yɛremfa wo din nhaw obi a ɔnyɛɛ bɔne.  
Akyiwadeɛ a ɛyɛ wo de, ma yɛnte ase na yɛnto so.

Agoo.  
Nana Bosom Pa, gye.  
Nana Bosom Pa, tie.  
Nana Bosom Pa, ma asomdwoe.

Yɛda wo ase.  
Ɛnyɛ dwoodwoo.  
Asomdwoe, asomdwoe, asomdwoe.

Sɛ yɛafom wɔ kasa mu, dwudwo yɛn ano.  
Sɛ yɛafom wɔ adwene mu, teɛ yɛn adwene.  
Sɛ yɛaka nea ɛnsɛ, ma ɛnsan nkɔ asomdwoe mu.  
Sɛ akyiwadeɛ bi atɔ mu a, ma yɛnyae ɔfrɛ yi wɔ fɛre ne obu mu; ma akɔmfoɔ mpaebɔ ne adwira nsiesie kwan no, na biribiara ntena ne sibea pa.  
Agoo.  
Yɛda wo ase.  
Ɛnyɛ dwoodwoo.

---

## Celestial Church

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

Hallelujah. Hallelujah. Hallelujah.  
Halleluyah, Halleluyah, Halleluyah.

O Lord God of Celestial Church of Christ, Father of our Lord Jesus Christ, receive our praise and thanksgiving.  
Let thy light be upon thy servants; let thy peace be upon the work of our hands.

Have mercy upon us, O God, according to thy lovingkindness: according unto the multitude of thy tender mercies blot out our transgressions.  
Wash us throughly from mine iniquity, and cleanse us from my sin.  
Create in us a clean heart, O God; and renew a right spirit within us.

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

Baba wa ti mbẹ li ọrun,  
Ki a bọ̀wọ̀ fun orúkọ rẹ.  
Ki ìjọba rẹ dé.  
Ti ìfẹ́ rẹ ni ki a ṣe ni ayé, bí ti ọrun.  
Fún wa li òní oúnjẹ wa ojoojúmọ́.  
Dárí gbèsè wa jì wa, bí awa ti ń dárí gbèsè àwọn onígbèsè wa jì wọ́n.  
Má sì fà wa sinu ìdánwò,  
ṣùgbọ́n gbà wa lọwọ ibi.  
Nítorí tirẹ ni ìjọba, àti agbára, àti ògo, lailai.  
Amin.

I lift up mine eyes unto the hills,  
from whence cometh my help.  
My help cometh from the LORD,  
which made heaven and earth.  
He will not suffer thy foot to be moved:  
he that keepeth thee will not slumber.  
Behold, he that keepeth Israel  
shall neither slumber nor sleep.  
The LORD is thy keeper:  
the LORD is thy shade upon thy right hand.  
The sun shall not smite thee by day,  
nor the moon by night.  
The LORD shall preserve thee from all evil:  
he shall preserve thy soul.  
The LORD shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in  
from this time forth, and even for evermore.

The LORD is my shepherd; I shall not want.  
He maketh me to lie down in green pastures:  
he leadeth me beside the still waters.  
He restoreth my soul:  
he leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name's sake.  
Yea, though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death,  
I will fear no evil:  
for thou art with me;  
thy rod and thy staff they comfort me.  
Thou preparest a table before me in the presence of mine enemies:  
thou anointest my head with oil;  
my cup runneth over.  
Surely goodness and mercy shall follow me all the days of my life:  
and I will dwell in the house of the LORD for ever.

O Lord Jesus Christ, Son of the living God, look upon this event with mercy.  
For 明日上线一切顺利，部署平安，无 P0 事故, let thy help and guidance stand.  
Let every preparation be ordered in wisdom; let every hand be steady; let every decision be clear.  
Let hidden faults be revealed before harm is done; let confusion be removed; let peace rule over the deployment.  
Preserve the going out and coming in of this work from this time forth.  
We seek success by thy mercy, not by the loss, dispossession, sickness, shortening of life, or downfall of any other person.  
Let obstacles be removed without harm; let responsibility, charity, and peace stand among all who labor.

Hallelujah. Hallelujah. Hallelujah.  
Halleluyah, Halleluyah, Halleluyah.

O Lord, receive thanksgiving from us.  
Keep this prayer under thy holy will, in cleanliness of heart, humility, and the order of thy Church.  
Let all be sealed in the name of our Lord Jesus Christ.  
Amen. Amen. Amen.

## Espiritismo Cruzado

En el nombre del Padre, y del Hijo, y del Espíritu Santo. Amén.

Dios todopoderoso, Padre de misericordia, ante tu presencia se pone esta oración por la salida a producción de mañana, para pedir luz, verdad, caridad, buen camino, serenidad en el despliegue y paz en todo lo que deba quedar funcionando.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua,  
sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum cotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Ave Maria, gratia plena, Dominus tecum;  
benedicta tu in mulieribus,  
et benedictus fructus ventris tui, Iesus.  
Sancta Maria, Mater Dei,  
ora pro nobis peccatoribus,  
nunc et in hora mortis nostrae. Amen.

Creo en Dios, Padre todopoderoso,  
Creador del cielo y de la tierra.  
Creo en Jesucristo, su único Hijo, nuestro Señor,  
que fue concebido por obra y gracia del Espíritu Santo,  
nació de Santa María Virgen,  
padeció bajo el poder de Poncio Pilato,  
fue crucificado, muerto y sepultado,  
descendió a los infiernos,  
al tercer día resucitó de entre los muertos,  
subió a los cielos  
y está sentado a la derecha de Dios, Padre todopoderoso.  
Desde allí ha de venir a juzgar a vivos y muertos.  
Creo en el Espíritu Santo,  
la santa Iglesia católica,  
la comunión de los santos,  
el perdón de los pecados,  
la resurrección de la carne  
y la vida eterna. Amén.

Con licencia de Dios, con licencia de los buenos espíritus, con licencia del cuadro espiritual de luz, se saluda a los mayores de luz, a los ancestros buenos y a los guías protectores que caminan con caridad.

Moyuba Olofi, moyuba Olodumare, moyuba Olorun.  
Moyuba eggun, moyuba ara onu.  
Moyuba mi ile, moyuba awon agba.  
Eleguá agó, Eleguá agó, Eleguá agó.  
Eshu Elegbara, Laroyé.

Ángel de la Guarda, dulce compañía, no desampares ni de noche ni de día; pon paz y alegría con todos los santos, Jesús, José y María.

Espíritus protectores, guías de luz, buenos muertos, misioneros espirituales y cordón de caridad, si es voluntad de Dios y por el bien de todos, atiendan esta súplica: que la salida a producción de mañana transcurra con orden, claridad y calma; que el despliegue sea seguro, estable y limpio; que no haya accidente P0, caída grave, pérdida, confusión ni perturbación injusta.

Ángel de la Guarda y guías protectores, acompañad este evento lícito; abrid camino recto, cerrad tropiezo injusto, sostened la mente, la palabra, las manos y el juicio técnico en paz. Que cada revisión sea clara, que cada alerta sea vista a tiempo, que cada decisión sea prudente, que el equipo actúe con paciencia, cooperación y responsabilidad.

Señor Dios, se pide éxito sin despojar a nadie, sin quitar bien ajeno, sin dañar el trabajo de otros, sin cargar culpa sobre inocentes y sin buscar ventaja injusta. Que todo bien recibido sea por camino limpio, con mérito, servicio y caridad.

Dios mío, si esta petición conviene al adelanto espiritual y al bien común, concédela por tu misericordia; si algo debe corregirse antes de avanzar, trae luz, señal clara, prudencia y entendimiento para atenderlo a tiempo.

Hermanos que sufrís, hermanos sin luz, hermanos confundidos, no se os manda ni se os desprecia; se os ofrece oración, caridad y camino. En nombre de Dios, recibid luz, dejad la perturbación, apartaos de este trabajo y seguid a los buenos guías que os conduzcan hacia la paz.

Padre nuestro que estás en el cielo,  
santificado sea tu Nombre;  
venga a nosotros tu Reino;  
hágase tu voluntad  
en la tierra como en el cielo.  
Danos hoy nuestro pan de cada día;  
perdona nuestras ofensas,  
como también nosotros perdonamos a los que nos ofenden;  
no nos dejes caer en la tentación,  
y líbranos del mal. Amén.

Dios te salve, María,  
llena eres de gracia;  
el Señor es contigo.  
Bendita tú eres entre todas las mujeres,  
y bendito es el fruto de tu vientre, Jesús.  
Santa María, Madre de Dios,  
ruega por nosotros pecadores,  
ahora y en la hora de nuestra muerte. Amén.

Eleguá agó, Eleguá agó, Eleguá agó.  
Laroyé, Laroyé, Laroyé.

A los buenos espíritus se les da gracias; a los muertos de luz se les da luz; a los guías se les da respeto; a Dios se le da gloria. Que toda inquietud quede elevada, toda sombra quede apartada por la luz de Dios, toda palabra quede en paz y todo camino quede cerrado sólo a la confusión, abierto sólo al bien permitido por Dios.

Paz para los vivos, luz para los muertos, caridad para todos.  
En el nombre del Padre, y del Hijo, y del Espíritu Santo. Amén.

---

## 马达加斯加 Famadihana

Ry Razana malala,  
Ry Razambenay ao amin’ny tranon-drazana,  
ry loharanon’ny anarana sy ny fihavanana,  
henoy izahay taranakareo.

Izahay taranaka mbola velona,  
mijoro amim-panajana sy fo madio,  
tsy hanadino anareo,  
tsy hanary ny lova,  
tsy hanapaka ny fihavanana.

Ry havanay efa nodimandry,  
anarana tsy very,  
ra tsy ritra,  
fahatsiarovana tsy maty,  
mipetraha am-piadanana ao amin’ny razana,  
ary aoka ny velona hahatsiaro amin-katsaram-panahy.

Ry Razana,  
izao no teninay:  
rahampitso misy asa lehibe,  
fametrahana sy fampandehanana ho an’ny asa an-tserasera,  
ka mangataka tsodrano izahay,  
mangataka fitahiana,  
mangataka saina mazava,  
mangataka lalana mahitsy.

Arovy ny asa sy ny olona miandraikitra azy,  
arovy ny teny, ny tanana, ny hevitra, ary ny fitaovana,  
aoka hilamina ny fametrahana,  
aoka handeha soa aman-tsara ny deployment,  
aoka tsy hisy P0,  
aoka tsy hisy loza lehibe,  
aoka ny sakana hiala tsy handratra olona.

Omeo fahendrena izahay hahita ny diso aloha,  
omeo fahatoniana izahay rehefa misy zavatra tsy ampoizina,  
omeo firaisan-kina izahay hifampandre sy hifanampy,  
omeo fiadanana ny asa, ny trano, ary ny saina.

Tsy mangataka soa amin’ny fanesorana ny anjaran’ny hafa izahay,  
tsy mangataka fandresena amin’ny fahavoazan’ny hafa izahay,  
fa mangataka soa madio,  
lalana marina,  
ary asa hahasoa tsy hanimba.

Aoka tsy hisy teny ratsy eo aminay,  
aoka tsy hisy fifandirana eo aminay,  
aoka tsy hisy fanadinoana ny andraikitra.  
Ny razana hajaina,  
ny velona hifankatia,  
ny asa hatao am-pahitsiana,  
ny taranaka hitohy amin’ny fihavanana.

Ry Razana,  
raiso ny fanajanay,  
raiso ny fahatsiarovanay,  
raiso ny teny entinay,  
ary omeo tsodrano izahay.

Tsodrano, tsodrano, tsodrano:  
ho mazava ny saina,  
ho tony ny fo,  
ho mahitsy ny lalana,  
ho voaaro ny asa,  
ho soa aman-tsara ny rahampitso.

Aoka tsy hihoatra ny tenin’ny loholona izahay,  
aoka tsy hanitsaka ny fomban-tany izahay,  
aoka tsy hikasika izay tsy anjaranay izahay,  
aoka ny fasana sy ny razana hohajaina amin’ny fahanginana sy fahamarinana.  
Mitoera am-piadanana, ry Razana.  
Izahay kosa hitahiry ny anarana,  
hitahiry ny fihavanana,  
hitahiry ny fanajana.

---

## 基库尤 Mungiki

Ngai wa Kĩrĩnyaga,  
Ngai wa Gĩkũyũ na Mũmbi,  
Thai, thathaiya Ngai, thai.

Ngai, nĩ tũrĩ haha,  
tũkũhoya na ngoro njega.  
Thai, thathaiya Ngai, thai.

Ngai, igua ihooya rĩitũ.  
Rora ũhoro wa rũciinĩ,  
rora wĩra wa gũtũma na gũkinyia andũ,  
rora njĩra ya deployment ĩkagĩa na thayũ,  
hatigakorwo na mũtino mũnene wa P0.  
Thai, thathaiya Ngai, thai.

Ngai, heana thayũ,  
heana ũiguano,  
heana ũthingu,  
heana ũtheri wa njĩra.  
Tũtireenda kũnyiita indo cia andũ angĩ,  
tũtireenda kũhinyia muoyo wa mũndũ o wothe;  
twenda wĩra ũthiĩ na ma, na thayũ, na ũtheri.  
Thai, thathaiya Ngai, thai.

Ngai wa Kĩrĩnyaga,  
Ngai wa maithe maitũ,  
Ngai wa maithe ma maithe maitũ,  
tũiguĩre, tũrathime, tũhe thayũ.  
Ihooya rĩĩ rĩgũe rĩna ũthingu, rĩna ũtheri, rĩtarĩ na hinya, rĩtarĩ na guoya, rĩtarĩ na kũhinyia mũndũ.  
Thai, thathaiya Ngai, thai.

## 约鲁巴 · Ifa / Òrìṣà 崇拜

Ìbà Olódùmarè.  
Ìbà Ilẹ̀.  
Ìbà Orí mi.  
Ìbà àwọn Egúngún ara òrun.  
Ìbà Èṣù Láàlú, Elegbára, onílé ọ̀nà, aláròyè.  
Ìbà Òrúnmìlà, Ẹlẹ́rìí ìpín.

Orí mi, àpẹrẹ.  
Orí mi, gbé mi.  
Orí mi, má ṣe mí.  
Orí mi, má gbàgbé mi.  
Orí mi, jẹ́ kí n rí ire.  
Orí mi, jẹ́ kí n kọjá ibi.

Òrúnmìlà, Ẹlẹ́rìí ìpín,  
Ìbikejì Olódùmarè,  
A-jé-jù-ogun,  
A-tún-orí-ti-kò-sùnwọ̀n ṣe,  
Ọlọ́gbọ́n tí ń mọ ọjọ́ ikú,  
Ọlọ́gbọ́n tí ń mọ ọjọ́ àìkú,  
Bàbá mi, Òrúnmìlà, gbọ́ ohùn mi.

A dúró níwájú rẹ̀ pẹ̀lú ìrẹ̀lẹ̀.  
A wá fún ìfilọ́lẹ̀ iṣẹ́ ọ̀la, kí ó lọ ní àlàáfíà, kí ìgbékalẹ̀ rẹ̀ dára, kí ìjàmbá P0 má ṣẹlẹ̀.  
Jẹ́ kí ire àṣeyọrí wọlé.  
Jẹ́ kí ibi ìdènà, ìdàrúdàpọ̀, aṣìṣe ńlá, àti ìjàmbá kúrò.  
Jẹ́ kí ọ̀nà ṣí fún gbogbo iṣẹ́ tó yẹ.  
Jẹ́ kí ọkàn balẹ̀, kí ọgbọ́n hàn, kí ọwọ́ ṣiṣẹ́ pẹ̀lú ìtójú.  
Jẹ́ kí Orí gba ire, kí ìwà pẹ̀lẹ́ bá iṣẹ́ lọ.  
A kò béèrè ire nípa jíjẹ́ kí ẹlòmíràn ṣòfò; a kò gba àṣeyọrí nípa fífi ẹlòmíràn ṣubú.  
Kí gbogbo ẹni tí ó ní ipa nínú iṣẹ́ yìí rí ìmọ̀lára, ìbáṣepọ̀ rere, àti ìpinnu tó dáa.

Mo dúpẹ́, Olódùmarè.  
Mo dúpẹ́, Orí mi.  
Mo dúpẹ́, àwọn Egúngún.  
Mo dúpẹ́, Èṣù Elegbára.  
Mo dúpẹ́, Òrúnmìlà.

Kí ọ̀rọ̀ wa dúró nínú òtítọ́ àti ìrẹ̀lẹ̀.  
Kí a má ṣe kọjá eewọ.  
Kí a má ṣe dá ohun tí a kò mọ̀ sílẹ̀.  
Kí Òrúnmìlà tọ́ ọ̀nà wa sí ọgbọ́n, ìwà pẹ̀lẹ́, àti àlàáfíà.

Àṣẹ.  
Àṣẹ.  
Àṣẹ.

---

## Mami Wata 信仰

We stand by clean water.  
Mami Wata, Mammy Water, Nne mmiri, Yeye Omi,  
we call only your name for this prayer.

Mami Wata o, Mami Wata o,  
bia, nuru olu anyị.  
Nne mmiri, nne oma,  
mmiri di ọcha, mmiri ndu.

Mammy Water, we hail you.  
Fine lady for water, mother for river,  
she wey sabi deep water,  
she wey hold mirror for truth,  
she wey cool hot heart.

Mami Wata o,  
for tomorrow go-live, for deployment wey dey come,  
make water clean, make road open,  
make bad mouth cool,  
make hand steady, make eye see true,  
make mind no scatter for night and morning.

Yeye Omi, iya omi,  
cover this work with white water.  
Omi tutu, omi alaafia,  
no fight, no lie, no confusion,  
no P0 wahala, no heavy accident,  
peace for system, peace for people,  
peace for every road wey the release go pass.

Mami Wata o, Mammy Water o,  
we no ask to take another person blessing,  
we no ask to cut another person life or luck.  
Make only clean success stand,  
make every hidden stone show for mirror,  
make every hot error cool before e burn.

Nne mmiri, carry bad thing go.  
Mmiri ndu, make heart dey quiet.  
If word no clear, make truth shine for water.  
If alarm rise, make wise hand answer am.  
If gate close, make safe road open.

Mami Wata o, no vex, no trouble.  
If we don speak wrong,  
make wrong word fall for water.  
If we don promise with mouth,  
make only true and clean promise stand.

We no call another spirit for this same mouth.  
We no force body, we no call possession,  
we no make sacrifice, we no make oath.  
Only Mami Wata name dey here,  
with clean water, cool heart, and peace.

Mmiri oma, kuru ihe ojoo laa.  
Mmiri ndu, mee ka obi di jụụ.  
Nne mmiri, receive this voice,  
receive this clean water,  
receive this word of peace.

Peace for water,  
peace for road,  
peace for house,  
peace for tomorrow deployment.  
Mammy Water, we thank you.  
Nne mmiri, daalu.  
Yeye Omi, mo dupe.  
Alaafia. Udo. Peace.

---

## Hoodoo / Rootwork

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Ghost. Amen.

I stand before the Most High God with clean speech and a steady heart.  
Let this prayer be for tomorrow’s launch: may the go-live be smooth, the deployment be safe, and no P0 incident arise.  
Let no falsehood, coercion, wrongful hand, or harm to the innocent be in it.  
Let this success take nothing unjustly from another: no bread from another table, no blessing stolen, no life shortened, no rightful work broken.

שִׁיר לַמַּעֲלוֹת אֶשָּׂא עֵינַי אֶל־הֶהָרִים מֵאַיִן יָבֹא עֶזְרִי׃  
עֶזְרִי מֵעִם יְהוָה עֹשֵׂה שָׁמַיִם וָאָרֶץ׃  
אַל־יִתֵּן לַמּוֹט רַגְלֶךָ אַל־יָנוּם שֹׁמְרֶךָ׃  
הִנֵּה לֹא־יָנוּם וְלֹא יִישָׁן שׁוֹמֵר יִשְׂרָאֵל׃  
יְהוָה שֹׁמְרֶךָ יְהוָה צִלְּךָ עַל־יַד יְמִינֶךָ׃  
יוֹמָם הַשֶּׁמֶשׁ לֹא־יַכֶּכָּה וְיָרֵחַ בַּלָּיְלָה׃  
יְהוָה יִשְׁמָרְךָ מִכָּל־רָע יִשְׁמֹר אֶת־נַפְשֶׁךָ׃  
יְהוָה יִשְׁמָר־צֵאתְךָ וּבוֹאֶךָ מֵעַתָּה וְעַד־עוֹלָם׃

Lord, keep the going out and the coming in of this work.  
Keep the hands steady, the minds clear, the checks true, the alerts quiet, and the road open.  
Let hidden faults be seen before harm is done.  
Let confusion be turned into order, delay into right timing, and pressure into calm judgment.  
Let every gate open cleanly, every service stand firm, every rollback path be ready, and every watcher be awake.

I speak no harm into the innocent.  
I bind no unwilling heart.  
I take back every crooked word, every proud demand, and every petition not fit to stand before God.

As my word is spoken before the Lord,  
let obstacles to a safe deployment be cut away.  
Let the road of tomorrow’s launch be opened in righteousness.  
Let the system be guarded from P0 failure, cascading harm, and unseen snares.  
Let the work be done by clean hands, sound counsel, and honest increase.  
Let all who depend on this work be kept in mercy and peace.

יֹשֵׁב בְּסֵתֶר עֶלְיוֹן בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן׃  
אֹמַר לַיהוָה מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי אֱלֹהַי אֶבְטַח־בּוֹ׃  
כִּי הוּא יַצִּילְךָ מִפַּח יָקוּשׁ מִדֶּבֶר הַוּוֹת׃  
בְּאֶבְרָתוֹ יָסֶךְ לָךְ וְתַחַת־כְּנָפָיו תֶּחְסֶה צִנָּה וְסֹחֵרָה אֲמִתּוֹ׃

Set this petition under the judgment of the Most High.  
What is righteous, establish it.  
What is crooked, remove it.  
What is not mine to command, return it to God.  
Let protection, reconciliation, clear roads, and right judgment stand around this event.

חָנֵּנִי אֱלֹהִים כְּחַסְדֶּךָ כְּרֹב רַחֲמֶיךָ מְחֵה פְשָׁעָי׃  
הֶרֶב כַּבְּסֵנִי מֵעֲוֹנִי וּמֵחַטָּאתִי טַהֲרֵנִי׃  
לֵב טָהוֹר בְּרָא־לִי אֱלֹהִים וְרוּחַ נָכוֹן חַדֵּשׁ בְּקִרְבִּי׃

By mercy, cleanse every fearful, harsh, or wrongful intention from this prayer.  
I withdraw any improper petition and release every demand that does not belong before God.  
Let the road be cleared, the work protected, the people reconciled, and the final judgment rest with the Lord.

Amen. Amen. Amen.

---

## Kimbanguism

Na nkombo ya Tata, ya Mwana mpe ya Molimo Mosantu. Amen.

Nzambi Tata, na miso na yo, biso bato na yo toyangani na motema moko mpo na likambo ya lobi: mise en ligne mpe déploiement ezala na kimia, na boyebi malamu, mpe na bokengi.  
Yesu Kristo, Nkolo na biso, yamba losambo oyo; Molimo Mosantu, tambwisa makanisi, maloba, maboko, mpe misala nyonso.

Bolingo.  
Mibeko.  
Misala.

Nkolo, toboyi kindoki, biloko ya nkisi, lokuta, koyina, koboma motema, mpe misala nyonso ya molili.  
Tika ete motema na biso ezala peto liboso na yo, mpe ete mosala oyo esalema na bosembo, na kimia, mpe na bolingo.  
Tosengi bolamu oyo kozanga kobotola bolamu ya basusu, kozanga kobebisa mosala ya basusu, mpe kozanga kotia moto moko na mpasi.

Tata na biso, ozali na likoló,  
nkombo na yo ezala mosantu,  
bokonzi na yo eya,  
mokano na yo esalema  
awa na mabele lokola na likoló.  
Pesa biso lelo bilei na biso ya mokolo.  
Limbisa biso masumu na biso,  
lokola biso mpe tolimbisaka baoyo basali biso mabe.  
Kotika biso te tokwea na komekama,  
kasi bikisa biso na moto mabe.  
Mpo na yo bokonzi, nguya mpe nkembo,  
libela na libela. Amen.

Nzembo 121:  
Nakotombola miso na ngai na bangomba:  
lisungi na ngai ekouta wapi?  
Lisungi na ngai ekouta epai ya Yawe,  
ye oyo asalaki likoló mpe mabele.  
Akotika lokolo na yo ekita te;  
mobateli na yo akolala pongi te.  
Tala, mobateli ya Isalaele  
akolala pongi te, akolala mpɔngi te.

Nkolo Nzambe, tala déploiement ya lobi.  
Pesa kimia na baoyo bakosala, pesa bokebi na baoyo bakotala, pesa bososoli na baoyo bakozwa mikano.  
Batela systèmes, réseaux, données, mpe bato nyonso oyo bakozwa litomba na mosala oyo.  
Sunga ete mise en ligne elekela malamu, ete makama minene ezala te, ete P0 accident ezala te, mpe ete soki mokakatano moke ebimi, ezwama noki, ebongisama na kimia, kozanga kobebisa bato.

Lendisa biso na Bolingo, mpo tóyokana malamu.  
Lendisa biso na Mibeko, mpo tólanda nzela ya sembo.  
Lendisa biso na Misala, mpo tólongisa mokumba na bosembo mpe na motema ya kimia.

Tika ete nyonso esalema na mokano na yo,  
na nkombo ya Yesu Kristo Nkolo na biso.  
Nkembo ezala na Tata, na Mwana, mpe na Molimo Mosantu,  
sik’oyo mpe libela na libela. Amen.

Nkolo, petola losambo na biso: tika tólanda Kristo kaka, tóbatela bomoi ya peto, tóboya kindoki, biloko ya nkisi, kobanga ya pamba, mpe lolendo.  
Tika kimia, bolingo, mibeko, mpe misala ya sembo etikala kati na biso. Amen.

---

## Aladura

Olúwa Ọlọ́run, Baba wa, Ọmọ, àti Ẹ̀mí Mímọ́, Ọba ògo, Ẹlẹ́dàá ọ̀run àti ayé,  
a dúpẹ́ fún àánú rẹ, fún ìmọ́lẹ̀ rẹ, fún ìtọ́sọ́nà rẹ, àti fún ìbáṣepọ̀ rẹ lórí iṣẹ́ tí yóò lọ síta ní ọ̀la.

Ní orúkọ Jésù Kristi Olúwa wa, a wá síwájú rẹ.  
A jẹ́wọ́ ẹ̀ṣẹ̀ wa, àìmọ̀ wa, ìgbéraga wa, ìbànújẹ wa, àti gbogbo ohun tí kò bá ìfẹ́ rẹ mu.  
Wẹ̀ wá mọ́, Olúwa; sọ ọkàn wa di mímọ́; jẹ́ kí ọwọ́ wa ṣiṣẹ́ ní òtítọ́, ní ìfarabalẹ̀, àti ní ọgbọ́n.

Ẹ̀mí Mímọ́, sọ̀kalẹ̀.  
Ẹ̀mí Mímọ́, tọ́ wa.  
Ẹ̀mí Mímọ́, ṣí ojú inú wa sí ohun tí a kò tíì rí, kí o sì mú ìmúrasílẹ̀, ìbáṣepọ̀, àti ìpinnu rere wá sínú gbogbo iṣẹ́ yìí.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

יֹשֵׁב בְּסֵתֶר עֶלְיוֹן  
בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן׃  
אֹמַר לַיהוָה מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי  
אֱלֹהַי אֶבְטַח־בּוֹ׃  
כִּי מַלְאָכָיו יְצַוֶּה־לָּךְ  
לִשְׁמָרְךָ בְּכָל־דְּרָכֶיךָ׃

Olúwa, gbọ́ àdúrà wa.  
Ìjọ Ọlọ́run, ẹ jẹ́ ká sọ pé: Olúwa, ṣàánú fún wa.  
Olúwa, ṣàánú fún wa.  
Jésù Kristi, jẹ́ ìmọ́lẹ̀ wa.  
Jésù Kristi, jẹ́ ìmọ́lẹ̀ wa.  
Ẹ̀mí Mímọ́, darí gbogbo ìgbésẹ̀.  
Ẹ̀mí Mímọ́, darí gbogbo ìgbésẹ̀.

Baba wa, a gbé ìfilọlẹ̀ ọ̀la lé ọ lọwọ.  
Jẹ́ kí deployment yìí lọ ní àlàáfíà, ní ìṣọ́ra, ní ìmúlò tó pé, àti ní ìbáṣepọ̀ rere.  
Dáàbò bo gbogbo eto, gbogbo data, gbogbo oníṣẹ́, gbogbo oníbàárà, àti gbogbo ọna tí iṣẹ́ yìí ń gba.  
Jẹ́ kí ìṣòro tó lè di P0 má bà a jẹ; jẹ́ kí ìkìlọ̀ tó yẹ hàn ní àsìkò; jẹ́ kí ọgbọ́n, sùúrù, àti ìfarabalẹ̀ wà lọ́dọ̀ gbogbo àwọn tí ń ṣiṣẹ́.  
Olúwa, mú ìtẹ̀síwájú wá láì pa ẹlòmíràn lára, láì gba ire ẹlòmíràn, láì sọ ẹnikẹ́ni di aláìní, àti láì din ìyè tàbí àlàáfíà ẹnikẹ́ni kù.

A kọ gbogbo òrìṣà, gbogbo òrò òkùnkùn, gbogbo òògùn ibi, gbogbo èké, gbogbo ẹ̀rù, àti gbogbo ìrònú ìpayà.  
A dúró nínú Jésù Kristi nìkan.  
Kì í ṣe agbára aṣọ, omi, epo, fitilà, agogo, tàbí ohun èlò kankan ni a gbẹ́kẹ̀lé; Olúwa, ìwọ nìkan ni ààbò wa àti ìrànlọ́wọ́ wa.

Ní orúkọ Jésù Kristi, a fi iṣẹ́ yìí sí abẹ́ ìfẹ́ Ọlọ́run.  
Kí ohun tí ó tọ́ ṣẹ; kí ohun tí kò tọ́ dá; kí ìmúlò rere, ìbáṣepọ̀ rere, àti àlàáfíà ṣẹ ní ọ̀la.  
A kò fi orúkọ Jésù bú ẹnikẹ́ni; a ń bẹ̀bẹ̀ pé kí ìdènà kúrò, kí ìmọ́lẹ̀ wọlé, kí àánú Ọlọ́run sì borí ìbẹ̀rù.

Baba, Ọmọ, àti Ẹ̀mí Mímọ́, gba ọpẹ́ wa; jẹ́ kí gbogbo ohun wà ní ìtẹríba sí ìfẹ́ rẹ mímọ́.  
Ní àánú rẹ, pa wá mọ́ nínú ìwà mímọ́, òtítọ́, ojúṣe, àti àlàáfíà; kí a má ṣe lo àdúrà fún ìbẹ̀rù, ìfipá múni, tàbí èrè àìtọ́.  
A fi gbogbo rẹ dì mọ́lẹ̀ ní orúkọ Jésù Kristi Olúwa wa.

Halleluyah. Halleluyah. Halleluyah.  
Àmín.

## Cherubim and Seraphim

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

Halleluyah.  
Halleluyah.  
Halleluyah.

Oluwa Ọlọrun Olódùmarè, Baba wa, a wá síwájú rẹ ní ìrẹ̀lẹ̀ àti ní ìgbàgbọ́.  
A jẹ́wọ́ ẹ̀ṣẹ̀ wa níwájú rẹ; wẹ̀ wa mọ́, sọ ọkàn wa di mímọ́, kí o sì tọ́ wa sí ọ̀nà ìmọ́lẹ̀ rẹ.

Baba wa ti mbẹ li ọrun,  
Ki a bọ̀wọ̀ fun orukọ rẹ;  
Ki ijọba rẹ de;  
Ifẹ tirẹ ni ki a ṣe ni aiye bi ti ọrun.  
Fun wa li oni onjẹ ojo wa.  
Dari ẹ̀ṣẹ̀ wa ji wa,  
bi awa ti dari ji awọn ti o ṣẹ̀ wa.  
Má ṣe fà wa sinu idanwo,  
ṣugbọn gbà wa lọwọ ibi.  
Nitori tirẹ ni ijọba, ati agbara, ati ogo, lailai. Amin.

Oluwa ni Olùṣọ́-àgùntàn wa; a kì yóò ṣaláìní.  
Ó ń tọ́ wa sí omi ìsinmi, ó ń tún ọkàn wa ṣe.  
Bí a tilẹ̀ ń rìn ní ojú-ọ̀nà ìdánwò, a kì yóò bẹ̀rù ibi, nítorí ìwọ wà pẹ̀lú wa.

A gbé ojú wa sókè sí òkè; láti ibo ni ìrànlọ́wọ́ wa yóò ti wá?  
Ìrànlọ́wọ́ wa wá láti ọ̀dọ̀ Oluwa, Ẹlẹ́dàá ọ̀run àti ayé.  
Oluwa, má jẹ́ kí ẹsẹ̀ wa yọ; má jẹ́ kí ẹni tí ń pa wa mọ́ sun.

Ẹmi Mimọ, sọ̀kalẹ̀.  
Ẹmi Mimọ, wá bá wa gbe.  
Ẹmi Mimọ, tọ́ ìrònú, ọwọ́, ọgbọ́n, àti iṣẹ́ wa sí ọ̀nà àlàáfíà.

Oluwa Jesu Kristi, ní orúkọ rẹ ni a gbé ìfilọlẹ̀ ọ̀la àti deployment wá síwájú rẹ.  
Jẹ́ kí gbogbo ohun lọ ní ìṣọ̀kan, ní ìtẹ́lọ́run, àti ní àlàáfíà.  
Jẹ́ kí ìmọ̀, ìfarabalẹ̀, ìtọ́sọ́nà, àti ìbáṣiṣẹ́ rere wà lórí gbogbo ìgbésẹ̀.  
Dá wa lójú ọ̀nà tó tọ́; ṣí ilẹ̀kùn ìmúdára; pa aṣìṣe tó lè fa ìjàmbá mọ́ kúrò níwájú wa.  
Kí ìṣẹ̀lẹ̀ P0 má ṣe dide; kí ìṣòro tó farahàn jẹ́ ẹni tí a lè rí, tí a lè lóye, tí a sì lè túnṣe ní àlàáfíà.

A kò béèrè ìrẹ̀lẹ̀ tàbí àṣeyọrí yìí láti gba ire ẹlòmíràn, láti pa ẹlòmíràn lára, tàbí láti dín ìbùkún ẹnikẹ́ni kù.  
Kí ire tó wá jẹ́ ire tó mọ́, ire tó dá lórí òtítọ́, iṣẹ́ rere, àti ìfẹ́ rẹ.

Ní orúkọ Jesu Kristi, a kéde pé ìbẹ̀rù kì yóò ṣàkóso wa.  
Àlàáfíà Kristi yóò ṣọ́ ọkàn wa; ọgbọ́n Ọlọrun yóò tọ́ ìpinnu wa; ìmọ́lẹ̀ Ẹmi Mimọ yóò ṣí ojú wa.  
Kí àwọn angẹli Oluwa ṣọ́ gbogbo ipa-ọ̀nà iṣẹ́ yìí, gẹ́gẹ́ bí ìfẹ́ Ọlọrun àti ní ìbámu pẹ̀lú òtítọ́ rẹ.

A dúpẹ́ lọwọ rẹ, Oluwa.  
A yin orúkọ rẹ.  
A fi gbogbo iṣẹ́ yìí lé ọ lọwọ, kì í ṣe nípa agbára wa, ṣùgbọ́n nípa àánú rẹ àti ìtọ́sọ́nà Ẹmi Mimọ.

Oluwa, pa wa mọ́ ní mímọ́, ní ìrònúpìwàdà, ní ìbágbọ́pọ̀, àti ní ìbẹ̀rù orúkọ rẹ.  
Jẹ́ kí adura wa dúró nínú ìmọ́lẹ̀ Kristi nìkan; jẹ́ kí ọkàn wa má ṣe rìn sí òkùnkùn, sí ìgbéraga, tàbí sí ìdàrúdàpọ̀.  
Kí gbogbo ohun tí a ṣe wà ní ìbámu pẹ̀lú ìfẹ́ rẹ, ní ìlànà rere, ní ìbòwọ̀ fún ìjọ, àti ní àlàáfíà fún gbogbo ènìyàn.

Amen.  
Halleluyah.  
Halleluyah.  
Halleluyah.
